Introduction
Welcome to the reference for the Lichess API! Lichess is free/libre, open-source chess server powered by volunteers and donations.

Get help in the Lichess Discord channel
API demo app with OAuth2 login and gameplay: source / demo
API UI app with OAuth2 login and endpoint forms: source / website
Contribute to this documentation on Github
Check out Lichess widgets to embed in your website
Download all Lichess rated games
Download all Lichess puzzles with themes, ratings and votes
Download all evaluated positions
Endpoint
All requests go to https://lichess.org (unless otherwise specified).

Clients
Python general API
MicroPython general API
Python general API - async
Python Lichess Bot
Python Board API for Certabo
Java general API
JavaScript & TypeScript general API
LichessNET - C# API Wrapper
Rate limiting
All requests are rate limited using various strategies, to ensure the API remains responsive for everyone. Only make one request at a time. If you receive an HTTP response with a 429 status, please wait a full minute before resuming API usage.

Streaming with ND-JSON
Some API endpoints stream their responses as Newline Delimited JSON a.k.a. nd-json, with one JSON object per line.

Here's a JavaScript utility function to help reading NDJSON streamed responses.

Authentication
Which authentication method is right for me?
Read about the Lichess API authentication methods and code examples

Personal Access Token
Personal API access tokens allow you to quickly interact with Lichess API without going through an OAuth flow.

Generate a personal access token
curl https://lichess.org/api/account -H "Authorization: Bearer {token}"
NodeJS example
Token Security
Keep your tokens secret. Do not share them in public repositories or public forums.
Your tokens can be used to make your account perform arbitrary actions (within the limits of the tokens' scope). You remain responsible for all activities on your account.
Do not hardcode tokens in your application's code. Use environment variables or a secure storage and ensure they are not shipped/exposed to users. Be especially careful that they are not included in frontend bundles or apps that are shipped to users.
If you suspect a token has been compromised, revoke it immediately.
To see your active tokens or revoke them, see your Personal API access tokens.

Authorization Code Flow with PKCE
The authorization code flow with PKCE allows your users to login with Lichess. Lichess supports unregistered and public clients (no client authentication, choose any unique client id). The only accepted code challenge method is S256. Access tokens are long-lived (expect one year), unless they are revoked. Refresh tokens are not supported.

See the documentation for the OAuth endpoints or the PKCE RFC for a precise protocol description.

Demo app
Minimal client-side example
Flask/Python example
Java example
NodeJS Passport strategy to login with Lichess OAuth2
Real life examples

Token format
Access tokens and authorization codes match ^[A-Za-z0-9_]+$. The length of tokens can be increased without notice. Make sure your application can handle at least 512 characters. By convention tokens have a recognizable prefix, but do not rely on this.

https://lichess.org

patronColorCopy link to patronColor
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
10
Players can choose a color for their Patron wings. See here for the color mappings.

The presence of this field indicates the player is an active Patron.

Set my kid mode status​Copy link
Set the kid mode status of the logged in user.

https://lichess.org/account/kid
Query Parameters
vCopy link to v
Type:boolean
required
Example
Kid mode status

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
ok
Type:boolean
required
Request Example forpost/api/account/kid
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/account/kid?v=true' \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN'

Test Request
(post /api/account/kid)
Status:200

{
  "ok": true
}
The kid mode status was set successfully for the logged in user.

Users ​Copy link
Access registered users on Lichess. https://lichess.org/player

Each user blog exposes an atom (RSS) feed, like https://lichess.org/@/thibault/blog.atom
User blogs mashup feed: https://lichess.org/blog/community.atom
User blogs mashup feed for a language: https://lichess.org/blog/community/fr.atom

Get real-time users status​Copy link
Read the online, playing and streaming flags of several users. This API is very fast and cheap on lichess side. So you can call it quite often (like once every 5 seconds). Use it to track players and know when they're connected on lichess and playing games.

Query Parameters
idsCopy link to ids
Type:string
required
Example
User IDs separated by commas. Up to 100 IDs.

withSignalCopy link to withSignal
Type:boolean
Example
Also return the network signal of the player, when available. It ranges from 1 (poor connection, lag > 500ms) to 4 (great connection, lag < 150ms) Defaults to false to preserve server resources.

withGameIdsCopy link to withGameIds
Type:boolean
Example
Also return the ID of the game being played, if any, for each player, in a playingId field. Defaults to false to preserve server resources.

withGameMetasCopy link to withGameMetas
Type:boolean
Example
Also return the id, time control and variant of the game being played, if any, for each player, in a playing field. Defaults to false to preserve server resources. Disables withGameIds.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:array object[]
Example
The list of users and their respective statuses.

id
Type:string
required
name
Type:string
required
flair
Type:string
See available flair list and images

online
Type:boolean
patron
Type:boolean
deprecated
Use patronColor value instead to determine if player is a patron.

patronColor
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
10
Players can choose a color for their Patron wings. See here for the color mappings.

The presence of this field indicates the player is an active Patron.

playing
Type:boolean
streaming
Type:boolean
title
Type:string
enum
only appears if the user is a titled player or a bot user

GM
WGM
IM
WIM
FM
Show all values
Request Example forget/api/users/status
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/users/status?ids=thibault%2Cmaia1%2Cmaia5&withSignal=true&withGameIds=true&withGameMetas=true'

Test Request
(get /api/users/status)
Status:200

[
  {
    "name": "Mary",
    "flair": "people.folded-hands-light-skin-tone",
    "patron": true,
    "patronColor": 1,
    "id": "mary"
  },
  {
    "name": "Ana",
    "title": "IM",
    "flair": "people.men-holding-hands-light-skin-tone",
    "id": "ana"
  }
]
The list of users and their respective statuses.

Get one leaderboard​Copy link
Get the leaderboard for a single speed or variant (a.k.a. perfType). There is no leaderboard for correspondence or puzzles. See https://lichess.org/player/top/200/bullet.

Path Parameters
nbCopy link to nb
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
200
required
Example
How many users to fetch

perfTypeCopy link to perfType
Type:string
enum
required
Example
The speed or variant

ultraBullet
bullet
blitz
rapid
classical
Show all values
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
users
Type:array TopUser[]
required
Show Child Attributesfor users
Request Example forget/api/player/top/{nb}/{perfType}
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/api/player/top/100/bullet

Test Request
(get /api/player/top/{nb}/{perfType})
Status:200

{
  "users": [
    {
      "id": "lola",

        "blitz": {
          "rating": 2452,
          "progress": 0
        }
      },
      "title": "IM",
      "patron": true,
      "patronColor": 1
    },
    {
      "id": "angel",
      "username": "Angel",
      "perfs": {
        "blitz": {
          "rating": 2421,
          "progress": 0
        }
      },
      "title": "IM"
    },
    {
      "id": "mei",
      "username": "Mei",
      "perfs": {
        "blitz": {
          "rating": 2376,
          "progress": 0
        }
      },
      "title": "GM"
    }
  ]
}
The list of top players for the variant.

Get user public data​Copy link
Read public data of a user.

Path Parameters
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
Query Parameters
trophiesCopy link to trophies
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include user trophies

profileCopy link to profile
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include user profile data

rankCopy link to rank
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include global lichess ranking for each perf

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Example
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
urlCopy link to url
Type:string
Format:uri
required
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
blockingCopy link to blocking
Type:boolean
only appears if the request is authenticated with OAuth2

countCopy link to count
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor count
createdAtCopy link to createdAt
Type:integer
Format:int64
Signed 64-bit integers (long type).

disabledCopy link to disabled
Type:boolean
only appears if a user's account is closed

flairCopy link to flair
Type:string
See available flair list and images

followableCopy link to followable
Type:boolean
only appears if the request is authenticated with OAuth2

followingCopy link to following
Type:boolean
only appears if the request is authenticated with OAuth2

patronCopy link to patron
Type:boolean
deprecated
Use patronColor value instead to determine if player is a patron.

patronColorCopy link to patronColor
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
10
Players can choose a color for their Patron wings. See here for the color mappings.

The presence of this field indicates the player is an active Patron.

perfsCopy link to perfs
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor perfs
playingCopy link to playing
Type:string
Format:uri
playTimeCopy link to playTime
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor playTime
profileCopy link to profile
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor profile
seenAtCopy link to seenAt
Type:integer
Format:int64
Signed 64-bit integers (long type).

streamerCopy link to streamer
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor streamer
streamingCopy link to streaming
Type:boolean
titleCopy link to title
Type:string
enum
only appears if the user is a titled player or a bot user

GM
WGM
IM
WIM
FM
Show all values
tosViolationCopy link to tosViolation
Type:boolean
only appears if a user's account is marked for the violation of Lichess TOS

verifiedCopy link to verified
Type:boolean
Request Example forget/api/user/{username}
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/user/{username}?trophies=false&profile=true&rank=false' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN'

Get rating history of a user​Copy link
Read rating history of a user, for all perf types. There is at most one entry per day. Format of an entry is [year, month, day, rating]. month starts at zero (January).

Path Parameters
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:array RatingHistoryEntry[]
Example
Example
The rating history of the user.

name
Type:string
points
Type:array array[]
Request Example forget/api/user/{username}/rating-history
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/user/{username}/rating-history'

The rating history of the user.

Get performance statistics of a user​Copy link
Read performance statistics of a user, for a single performance. Similar to the performance pages on the website.

Path Parameters
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
perfCopy link to perf
Type:string
enum
required
ultraBullet
bullet
blitz
rapid
classical
Show all values
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
percentile
Type:number
required
perf
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor perf
rank
Type:integer | null
required
stat
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor stat
user
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor user
Request Example forget/api/user/{username}/perf/{perf}
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/user/{username}/perf/ultraBullet'

Get user activity​Copy link
Read data to generate the activity feed of a user.

Path Parameters
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:array UserActivity[]
Example
The activity feed of the user.

Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor interval

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor correspondenceEnds

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor correspondenceMoves

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor follows

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor games

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor patron

Type:array object[]
Show Child Attributesfor posts

Type:array object[]
Show Child Attributesfor practice

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor puzzles

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor racer

Type:array string[]

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor storm

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor streak

Type:boolean

Show Child Attributesfor studies

Type:array object[]
Show Child Attributesfor teams

Show Child Attributesfor tournaments

Get users by ID​Copy link
Get up to 300 users by their IDs. Users are returned in the same order as the IDs. The method is POST to allow a longer list of IDs to be sent in the request body. Please do not try to download all the Lichess users with this endpoint, or any other endpoint. An API is not a way to fully export a website. We do not provide a full download of the Lichess users. This endpoint is limited to 8,000 users every 10 minutes, and 120,000 every day.

Query Parameters
profileCopy link to profile
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include user profile data

rankCopy link to rank
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include global lichess ranking for each perf

Body
required
text/plain
User IDs separated by commas.

Type:string
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:array User[]
Example
The list of users.

id
Type:string
required
username
Type:string
required
createdAt
Type:integer
Format:int64
Signed 64-bit integers (long type).

disabled
Type:boolean
only appears if a user's account is closed

flair
Type:string
See available flair list and images

patron
Type:boolean
deprecated
Use patronColor value instead to determine if player is a patron.

patronColor
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
10
Players can choose a color for their Patron wings. See here for the color mappings.

The presence of this field indicates the player is an active Patron.

perfs
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor perfs
playTime
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor playTime
profile
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor profile
seenAt
Type:integer
Format:int64
Signed 64-bit integers (long type).

title
Type:string
enum
only appears if the user is a titled player or a bot user

GM
WGM
IM
WIM
FM
Show all values
tosViolation
Type:boolean
only appears if a user's account is marked for the violation of Lichess TOS

verified
Type:boolean
Request Example forpost/api/users
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/users?profile=true&rank=false' \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: text/plain' \
  --data '"thibault,maia1,maia5"'

Test Request
(post /api/users)
Status:200

[
  {
    "id": "thibault",
    "username": "thibault",
    "perfs": {
      "ultraBullet": {

Get live streamers​Copy link
Get basic info about currently streaming users. This API is very fast and cheap on lichess side. So you can call it quite often (like once every 5 seconds).

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:array object[]
Example
The list of live streamers and their respective information.

Type:object
id
Type:string
required
name
Type:string
required
flair
Type:string
See available flair list and images

patron
Type:boolean
deprecated
Use patronColor value instead to determine if player is a patron.

patronColor
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
10
Players can choose a color for their Patron wings. See here for the color mappings.

The presence of this field indicates the player is an active Patron.

stream
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor stream
streamer
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor streamer
title
Type:string
enum
only appears if the user is a titled player or a bot user

WGM
IM
WIM
FM
Show all values

Get crosstable​Copy link
Get total number of games, and current score, of any two users. If the matchup flag is provided, and the users are currently playing, also gets the current match game number and scores.

Path Parameters
user1Copy link to user1
Type:string
required
user2Copy link to user2
Type:string
required
Query Parameters
matchupCopy link to matchup
Type:boolean
Whether to get the current match data, if any

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
Example
nbGames
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

users
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor users
Request Example forget/api/crosstable/{user1}/{user2}
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/crosstable/{user1}/{user2}?matchup=true'

Test Request
(get /api/crosstable/{user1}/{user2})
Status:200

{
  "users": {
    "drnykterstein": 753.5,
    "rebeccaharris": 459.5
  },
  "nbGames": 1213
}
The crosstable of the two users.

Autocomplete usernames​Copy link
Provides autocompletion options for an incomplete username.

Query Parameters
termCopy link to term
Type:string
min length:  
3
required
The beginning of a username

existsCopy link to exists
Type:boolean
default: 
false
If true, only checks if the user exists.

objectCopy link to object
Type:boolean
default: 
false
false returns an array of usernames
true returns an object with matching users
namesCopy link to names
Type:boolean
default: 
false
false returns an array of usernames
true returns an array of usernames with preferred casing
friendCopy link to friend
Type:boolean
Returns followed players matching term if any, else returns other players. Requires OAuth.

teamCopy link to team
Type:string
Search within a team. Use team ID/slug.

tourCopy link to tour
Type:string
Search within a arena tournament. Use tournament ID.

swissCopy link to swiss
Type:string
Search within a Swiss tournament.

teacherCopy link to teacher
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Only search for players who also have a teacher role.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
An array of players which usernames start with the provided term.


One of
array string[]
Type:array string[]
Request Example forget/api/player/autocomplete
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/player/autocomplete?term=&exists=false&object=false&names=false&friend=true&team=&tour=&swiss=&teacher=false' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN'

Test Request
(get /api/player/autocomplete)
Status:200

[
  "bobby"
]
An array of players which usernames start with the provided term.


list of usernames
Add a note for a user​Copy link
Add a private note available only to you about this account.

Path Parameters
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
Example
Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
textCopy link to text
Type:string
required
The contents of the note

Responses
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
ok
Type:boolean
required
Request Example forpost/api/user/{username}/note
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/api/user/thibault/note \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'text='

Test Request
(post /api/user/{username}/note)
Status:200

{
  "ok": true
}
The note was successfully added.

Type:string
required
Example
Responses
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
ok
Type:boolean
required

Export one game​Copy link
Download one game in either PGN or JSON format. Ongoing games are delayed by a few seconds ranging from 3 to 60 depending on the time control, as to prevent cheat bots from using this API.

Path Parameters
gameIdCopy link to gameId
Type:string
min length:  
8
max length:  
8
required
The game ID

Query Parameters
movesCopy link to moves
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN moves.

pgnInJsonCopy link to pgnInJson
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the full PGN within the JSON response, in a pgn field.

tagsCopy link to tags
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN tags.

clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include clock status when available. Either as PGN comments: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] } Or in a clocks JSON field, as centisecond integers, depending on the response type.

evalsCopy link to evals
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include analysis evaluations and comments, when available. Either as PGN comments: 12. Bxf6 { [%eval 0.23] } a3 { [%eval -1.09] } Or in an analysis JSON field, depending on the response type.

accuracyCopy link to accuracy
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include accuracy percent of each player, when available. Only available in JSON.

openingCopy link to opening
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the opening name. Example: [Opening "King's Gambit Accepted, King's Knight Gambit"]

divisionCopy link to division
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Plies which mark the beginning of the middlegame and endgame. Only available in JSON

literateCopy link to literate
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Insert textual annotations in the PGN about the opening, analysis variations, mistakes, and game termination. Example: 5... g4? { (-0.98 → 0.60) Mistake. Best move was h6. } (5... h6 6. d4 Ne7 7. g3 d5 8. exd5 fxg3 9. hxg3 c6 10. dxc6)

withBookmarkedCopy link to withBookmarked
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Add a bookmarked: true JSON field when the logged in user has bookmarked the game. The response type must be set to application/x-ndjson by the request Accept header.

Headers
AcceptCopy link to Accept
Type:string
enum
default: 
"application/x-chess-pgn"
Specify the desired response format. Use application/x-chess-pgn to get the games in PGN format. Use application/json to get the games in JSON format.

application/x-chess-pgn
application/json
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
Example
The game representation.

Request Example forget/game/export/{gameId}
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/game/export/{gameId}?moves=true&pgnInJson=false&tags=true&clocks=true&evals=true&accuracy=false&opening=true&division=true&literate=false&withBookmarked=false' \
  --header 'Accept: application/x-chess-pgn'

The game representation.

Export ongoing game of a user​Copy link
Download the ongoing game, or the last game played, of a user. Available in either PGN or JSON format. Ongoing games are delayed by a few seconds ranging from 3 to 60 depending on the time control, as to prevent cheat bots from using this API.

Path Parameters
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
Query Parameters
movesCopy link to moves
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN moves.

pgnInJsonCopy link to pgnInJson
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the full PGN within the JSON response, in a pgn field.

tagsCopy link to tags
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN tags.

clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include clock status when available. Either as PGN comments: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] } Or in a clocks JSON field, as centisecond integers, depending on the response type.

evalsCopy link to evals
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include analysis evaluations and comments, when available. Either as PGN comments: 12. Bxf6 { [%eval 0.23] } a3 { [%eval -1.09] } Or in an analysis JSON field, depending on the response type.

accuracyCopy link to accuracy
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include accuracy percent of each player, when available. Only available in JSON.

openingCopy link to opening
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the opening name. Example: [Opening "King's Gambit Accepted, King's Knight Gambit"]

divisionCopy link to division
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Plies which mark the beginning of the middlegame and endgame. Only available in JSON

literateCopy link to literate
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Insert textual annotations in the PGN about the opening, analysis variations, mistakes, and game termination. Example: 5... g4? { (-0.98 → 0.60) Mistake. Best move was h6. } (5... h6 6. d4 Ne7 7. g3 d5 8. exd5 fxg3 9. hxg3 c6 10. dxc6)

Headers
AcceptCopy link to Accept
Type:string
enum
default: 
"application/x-chess-pgn"
Specify the desired response format. Use application/x-chess-pgn to get the games in PGN format. Use application/json to get the games in JSON format.

application/x-chess-pgn
application/json
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
The ongoing (or last) game of a user.

Request Example forget/api/user/{username}/current-game

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/user/{username}/current-game?moves=true&pgnInJson=false&tags=true&clocks=true&evals=true&accuracy=false&opening=true&division=false&literate=false' \
  --header 'Accept: application/x-chess-pgn'

The ongoing (or last) game of a user.

Export games of a user​Copy link
Download all games of any user in PGN or ndjson format. Games are sorted by reverse chronological order (most recent first). We recommend streaming the response, for it can be very long. https://lichess.org/@/german11 for instance has more than 500,000 games. The game stream is throttled, depending on who is making the request:

Anonymous request: 20 games per second
OAuth2 authenticated request: 30 games per second
Authenticated, downloading your own games: 60 games per second
Path Parameters
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
The user name.

Query Parameters
sinceCopy link to since
Type:integer
min:  
1356998400070
Download games played since this timestamp. Defaults to account creation date.

untilCopy link to until
Type:integer
min:  
1356998400070
Download games played until this timestamp. Defaults to now.

maxCopy link to max
Type:integer
min:  
1
How many games to download. Leave empty to download all games.

vsCopy link to vs
Type:string
[Filter] Only games played against this opponent

ratedCopy link to rated
Type:boolean
[Filter] Only rated (true) or casual (false) games

perfTypeCopy link to perfType
Type:string
enum
[Filter] Only games in these speeds or variants. Multiple perf types can be specified, separated by a comma. Example: blitz,rapid,classical

ultraBullet
bullet
blitz
rapid
classical
Show all values
colorCopy link to color
Type:string
enum
[Filter] Only games played as this color.

white
black
analysedCopy link to analysed
Type:boolean
[Filter] Only games with or without a computer analysis available

movesCopy link to moves
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN moves.

pgnInJsonCopy link to pgnInJson
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the full PGN within the JSON response, in a pgn field. The response type must be set to application/x-ndjson by the request Accept header.

tagsCopy link to tags
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN tags.

clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include clock status when available. Either as PGN comments: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] } Or in a clocks JSON field, as centisecond integers, depending on the response type.

evalsCopy link to evals
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include analysis evaluations and comments, when available. Either as PGN comments: 12. Bxf6 { [%eval 0.23] } a3 { [%eval -1.09] } Or in an analysis JSON field, depending on the response type.

accuracyCopy link to accuracy
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include accuracy percent of each player, when available. Only available in JSON.

openingCopy link to opening
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the opening name. Example: [Opening "King's Gambit Accepted, King's Knight Gambit"]

divisionCopy link to division
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Plies which mark the beginning of the middlegame and endgame. Only available in JSON

ongoingCopy link to ongoing
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Ongoing games are delayed by a few seconds ranging from 3 to 60 depending on the time control, as to prevent cheat bots from using this API.

finishedCopy link to finished
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include finished games. Set to false to only get ongoing games.

literateCopy link to literate
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Insert textual annotations in the PGN about the opening, analysis variations, mistakes, and game termination. Example: 5... g4? { (-0.98 → 0.60) Mistake. Best move was h6. } (5... h6 6. d4 Ne7 7. g3 d5 8. exd5 fxg3 9. hxg3 c6 10. dxc6)

lastFenCopy link to lastFen
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the X-FEN notation of the last position of the game. The response type must be set to application/x-ndjson by the request Accept header.

withBookmarkedCopy link to withBookmarked
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Add a bookmarked: true JSON field when the logged in user has bookmarked the game. The response type must be set to application/x-ndjson by the request Accept header.

sortCopy link to sort
Type:string
enum
default: 
"dateDesc"
Sort order of the games.

dateAsc
dateDesc
Headers
AcceptCopy link to Accept
Type:string
enum
default: 
"application/x-chess-pgn"
Specify the desired response format. Use application/x-chess-pgn to get the games in PGN format. Use application/x-ndjson to get the games in ndjson format. Read about ndjson here and how you can parse it in Javascript.

application/x-chess-pgn
application/x-ndjson
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
The games of the user.

Export games by IDs​Copy link
Download games by IDs in PGN or ndjson format, depending on the request Accept header. Games are sorted by reverse chronological order (most recent first) The method is POST so a longer list of IDs can be sent in the request body. 300 IDs can be submitted. Ongoing games are delayed by a few seconds ranging from 3 to 60 depending on the time control, as to prevent cheat bots from using this API.

Query Parameters
movesCopy link to moves
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN moves.

pgnInJsonCopy link to pgnInJson
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the full PGN within the JSON response, in a pgn field.

tagsCopy link to tags
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN tags.

clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include clock status when available. Either as PGN comments: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] } Or in a clocks JSON field, as centisecond integers, depending on the response type.

evalsCopy link to evals
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include analysis evaluations and comments, when available. Either as PGN comments: 12. Bxf6 { [%eval 0.23] } a3 { [%eval -1.09] } Or in an analysis JSON field, depending on the response type.

accuracyCopy link to accuracy
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include accuracy percent of each player, when available. Only available in JSON.

openingCopy link to opening
Type:boolean
default:

divisionCopy link to division
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Plies which mark the beginning of the middlegame and endgame. Only available in JSON

literateCopy link to literate
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Insert textual annotations in the PGN about the opening, analysis variations, mistakes, and game termination. Example: 5... g4? { (-0.98 → 0.60) Mistake. Best move was h6. } (5... h6 6. d4 Ne7 7. g3 d5 8. exd5 fxg3 9. hxg3 c6 10. dxc6)

Headers

Stream games of users​Copy link
Stream the games played between a list of users, in real time. Only games where both players are part of the list are included. The stream emits an event each time a game is started or finished. To also get all current ongoing games at the beginning of the stream, use the withCurrentGames flag. Games are streamed as ndjson. Maximum number of users: 300. The method is POST so a longer list of IDs can be sent in the request body.

Query Parameters
withCurrentGamesCopy link to withCurrentGames
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the already started games at the beginning of the stream.

Body
required
text/plain
Up to 300 user IDs separated by commas. Example: thibault,maia1,maia5

Type:string
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:array GameStreamGame[]
Example
The stream of the games played between the users.

Stream games by IDs​Copy link
Creates a stream of games from an arbitrary streamId, and a list of game IDs. The stream first outputs the games that already exists, then emits an event each time a game is started or finished. Games are streamed as ndjson. Maximum number of games: 500 for anonymous requests, or 1000 for OAuth2 authenticated requests. While the stream is open, it is possible to add new game IDs to watch.

Path Parameters
streamIdCopy link to streamId
Type:string
required
Example
Arbitrary stream ID that you can later use to add game IDs to the stream.

Body
required
text/plain
Up to 500 or 1000 game IDs separated by commas. Example: gameId01,gameId02,gameId03

Type:string
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:array GameStreamGame[]

Stream moves of a game​Copy link
Stream positions and moves of any ongoing game, in ndjson. A description of the game is sent as a first message. Then a message is sent each time a move is played. Finally, a description of the game is sent when it finishes, and the stream is closed. Ongoing games are delayed by a few seconds ranging from 3 to 60 depending on the time control, as to prevent cheat bots from using this API. No more than 8 game streams can be opened at the same time from the same IP address.

Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
Example
Responses
200Copy link to 200
Type:array object[]
Example
The stream of the game moves.

Import one game​Copy link
Import a game from PGN. See https://lichess.org/paste. Rate limiting: 200 games per hour for OAuth requests, 100 games per hour for anonymous requests. To broadcast ongoing games, consider pushing to a broadcast instead. To analyse a position or a line, just construct an analysis board URL (most standard tags supported if URL-encoded): https://lichess.org/analysis/pgn/e4_e5_Nf3_Nc6_Bc4_Bc5_Bxf7+

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
A single game to import

pgnCopy link to pgn
Type:string
The PGN. It can contain only one game. Most standard tags are supported.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
id
Type:string
Example
The game ID

url
Type:string
Format:uri
The game URL

Request Example forpost/api/import
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/api/import \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'pgn='

Test Request
(post /api/import)
Status:200

{
  "id": "R6iLjwz5",
  "url": "https://lichess.org/R6iLjwz5"
}
The game was successfully imported.

O-O { [%clk 0:02:47] } O-O { [%clk 0:02:45] } 8. b3 { [%clk 0:02:45] } d5 { [%clk 0:02:45] } 9. exd5 { [%clk 0:02:33] } cxd5 { [%clk 0:02:40] } 10. Nxe5 { [%clk 0:02:31] } Qd6 { [%clk 0:02:38] } 1-0
Imported games in PGN format

Export your bookmarked games​Copy link
Download all games bookmarked by you, in PGN or ndjson format. Games are sorted by reverse chronological order (most recent first). We recommend streaming the response, for it can be very long.

Query Parameters
sinceCopy link to since
Type:integer
min:  
1356998400070
Download games bookmarked since this timestamp. Defaults to account creation date.

untilCopy link to until
Type:integer
min:  
1356998400070
Download games bookmarked until this timestamp. Defaults to now.

maxCopy link to max
Type:integer
min:  
1
How many bookmarked games to download. Leave empty to download all bookmarked games.

movesCopy link to moves
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN moves.

pgnInJsonCopy link to pgnInJson
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the full PGN within the JSON response, in a pgn field. The response type must be set to application/x-ndjson by the request Accept header.

tagsCopy link to tags
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN tags.

clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include clock status when available. Either as PGN comments: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] } Or in a clocks JSON field, as centisecond integers, depending on the response type.

evalsCopy link to evals
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include analysis evaluations and comments, when available. Either as PGN comments: 12. Bxf6 { [%eval 0.23] } a3 { [%eval -1.09] } Or in an analysis JSON field, depending on the response type.

accuracyCopy link to accuracy
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include accuracy percent of each player, when available. Only available in JSON.

openingCopy link to opening
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the opening name. Example: [Opening "King's Gambit Accepted, King's Knight Gambit"]

divisionCopy link to division
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Plies which mark the beginning of the middlegame and endgame. Only available in JSON

literateCopy link to literate
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Insert textual annotations in the PGN about the opening, analysis variations, mistakes, and game termination. Example: 5... g4? { (-0.98 → 0.60) Mistake. Best move was h6. } (5... h6 6. d4 Ne7 7. g3 d5 8. exd5 fxg3 9. hxg3 c6 10. dxc6)

lastFenCopy link to lastFen
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the X-FEN notation of the last position of the game. The response type must be set to application/x-ndjson by the request Accept header.

sortCopy link to sort
Type:string
enum
default: 
"dateDesc"
Sort order of the bookmarks.

dateAsc
dateDesc
Headers
AcceptCopy link to Accept
Type:string
enum
default: 
"application/x-chess-pgn"
Specify the desired response format. Use application/x-chess-pgn to get the games in PGN format. Use application/x-ndjson to get the games in ndjson format. Read about ndjson here and how you can parse it in Javascript.

application/x-chess-pgn
application/x-ndjson
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
The bookmarked games of the user.

Request Example forget/api/games/export/bookmarks
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/games/export/bookmarks?since=1356998400070&until=1356998400070&max=1&moves=true&pgnInJson=false&tags=true&clocks=false&evals=false&accuracy=false&opening=false&division=false&literate=false&lastFen=false&sort=dateDesc' \
  --header 'Accept: application/x-chess-pgn' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN'

featured
d
Type:featured
required
The data of the message

Show featuredfor d
t
const:  
featured
required
The type of message. A summary of the game is sent as the first message and when the featured game changes. Subsequent messages are just the X-FEN, last move, and clocks.

Get best ongoing games of a TV channel​Copy link
Get a list of ongoing games for a given TV channel. Similar to lichess.org/games. Available in PGN or ndjson format, depending on the request Accept header.

Path Parameters
channelCopy link to channel
Type:string
required
The name of the channel in camel case.

Query Parameters
nbCopy link to nb
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
30
default: 
10
Number of games to fetch.

movesCopy link to moves
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN moves.

pgnInJsonCopy link to pgnInJson
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the full PGN within the JSON response, in a pgn field.

tagsCopy link to tags
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN tags.

clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include clock status when available. Either as PGN comments: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] } Or in a clocks JSON field, as centisecond integers, depending on the response type.

openingCopy link to opening
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the opening name. Example: [Opening "King's Gambit Accepted, King's Knight Gambit"]

Headers
AcceptCopy link to Accept
Type:string
enum
default: 
"application/x-chess-pgn"
Specify the desired response format. Use application/x-chess-pgn to get the games in PGN format. Use application/x-ndjson to get the games in ndjson format. Read about ndjson here and how you can parse it in Javascript.

application/x-chess-pgn
application/x-ndjson
Responses
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
Example
The representation of the games.

Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/tv/{channel}?nb=10&moves=true&pgnInJson=false&tags=true&clocks=false&opening=false' \
  --header 'Accept: application/x-chess-pgn'

Get a new puzzle​Copy link
Get a random Lichess puzzle in JSON format.

If authenticated, only returns puzzles that the user has never seen before.

DO NOT use this endpoint to enumerate puzzles for mass download. Instead, download the full public puzzle database.

Query Parameters
angleCopy link to angle
Type:string
The theme or opening to filter puzzles with.

Available themes are listed in the lichess source code and the lichess training themes hyperlinks.

difficultyCopy link to difficulty
Type:string

Get multiple puzzles at once​Copy link
Get a batch of random Lichess puzzles in JSON format.

If authenticated, only returns puzzles that the user has never seen before.

DO NOT use this endpoint to enumerate puzzles for mass download. Instead, download the full public puzzle database.

Path Parameters
angleCopy link to angle
Type:string
required
Example
The theme or opening to filter puzzles with. Recommended: mix.

Available themes are listed in the lichess source code and the lichess training themes hyperlinks.

Query Parameters
difficultyCopy link to difficulty
Type:string
enum
The desired puzzle difficulty, relative to the authenticated user puzzle rating, or 1500 if anonymous.

easiest
easier
normal
harder
hardest
nbCopy link to nb
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
50
default: 
15
Example
How many puzzles to fetch. Just set it to 1 if you only need one puzzle.

colorCopy link to color
Type:string
enum
The color to play. Better left empty to automatically get 50% white. Currently only works when nb=1.

white
black
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
glicko
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor glicko
puzzles
Type:array PuzzleAndGame[]
Show Child Attributesfor puzzles
Request Example forget/api/puzzle/batch/{angle}
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/puzzle/batch/mix?difficulty=easiest&nb=10&color=white' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN'

Solve multiple puzzles at once​Copy link
Set puzzles as solved and update ratings.

Path Parameters
angleCopy link to angle
Type:string
required
Example
The theme or opening of the solved puzzles.

Available themes are listed in the lichess source code and the lichess training themes hyperlinks.

Query Parameters
nbCopy link to nb
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
50
default: 
0
Example
When > 0, the response includes a new puzzle batch with that many puzzles.

This is equivalent to calling /api/puzzle/batch/{angle}, and can sometimes save a request.

Body
required
application/json
List of solved puzzles

solutionsCopy link to solutions
Type:array object[]
Show Child Attributesfor solutions
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
glicko
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor glicko
puzzles
Type:array PuzzleAndGame[]
Show Child Attributesfor puzzles
rounds
Type:array object[]
Show Child Attributesfor rounds
Request Example forpost/api/puzzle/batch/{angle}
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/puzzle/batch/mix?nb=1' \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data '{
  "solutions": [
    {
      "id": "",
      "win": true,
      "rated": true
    }
  ]
}'

Get your puzzle activity​Copy link
Download your puzzle activity in ndjson format. Puzzle activity is sorted by reverse chronological order (most recent first) We recommend streaming the response, for it can be very long.

Query Parameters
maxCopy link to max
Type:integer
min:  
1
How many entries to download. Leave empty to download all activity.

beforeCopy link to before
Type:integer
min:  
1356998400070
Download entries before this timestamp. Defaults to now. Use before and max for pagination.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
date
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

puzzle
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor puzzle
win
Type:boolean
required
Request Example forget/api/puzzle/activity
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/puzzle/activity?max=1&before=1356998400070' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN'

Test Request
(get /api/puzzle/activity)
Status:200

  "date": 1764375040769,

    "plays": 8294,

      "b7h1",
      "e1d2",
      "h1b1",
      "b3b1",

    "lastMove": "c1b1"

Get puzzles to replay​Copy link
Gets the puzzle IDs of remaining puzzles to re-attempt in JSON format.

Type:integer
required
How many days to look back when aggregating puzzle results. 30 is sensible.

Type:string
required
The theme or opening to filter puzzles with.

Type:object

Create and join a puzzle race​Copy link
Create a new private puzzle race. The Lichess user who creates the race must join the race page, and manually start the race when enough players have joined.

https://lichess.org/racer
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
id
Type:string
required
url
Type:string
Format:uri
required

  --request POST \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN'

  "url": "https://lichess.org/racer/3ULiM"

The new puzzle race.

Get puzzle race results​Copy link
Get the results of a puzzle race. Returns information about players, puzzles, and the current status of the race.

https://lichess.org/racer
Note that Lichess puzzle races are not persisted, and are only available for 30 minutes. After that delay, they are permanently deleted.

Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
The puzzle race ID

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
finishesAt
Type:integer
required
Timestamp in milliseconds when the race finishes

id
Type:string
required
Unique identifier of the puzzle race

owner
Type:string
required
Owner of the puzzle race

players
Type:array object[]
required
List of players participating in the race

Show Child Attributesfor players
puzzles
Type:array object[]
required
List of puzzles in the race

Show Child Attributesfor puzzles
startsAt
Type:integer
required
Timestamp in milliseconds when the race started

404Copy link to 404
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required

Teams ​Copy link

Get team swiss tournaments​Copy link
Get all swiss tournaments of a team. Tournaments are sorted by reverse chronological order of start date (last starting first). Tournaments are streamed as ndjson.

Path Parameters
teamIdCopy link to teamId
Type:string
required
Example
Query Parameters
maxCopy link to max
Type:integer
min:  
1
default: 
100
How many tournaments to download.

statusCopy link to status
Type:string
enum
[Filter] Only swiss tournaments in this current state.

created
started
finished
createdByCopy link to createdBy
Type:string
[Filter] Only swiss tournaments created by a given user.

nameCopy link to name
Type:string
[Filter] Only swiss tournaments with a given name.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
clock
Type:object
required

Type:string
required

Type:string
required

Type:string
required

Type:number
required

Type:number
required

Type:number
required

Type:boolean
required

Type:number
required
startsAt
Type:string
required
status
Type:string
enum
required
The current state of the swiss tournament

created
started
finished
variant
Type:string
required
verdicts
Type:object
required

nextRound
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor nextRound

Show Child Attributesfor stats
Request Example forget/api/team/{teamId}/swiss
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/team/coders/swiss?max=100&status=created&createdBy=&name='

Get members of a team​Copy link
Members are sorted by reverse chronological order of joining the team (most recent first). OAuth is only required if the list of members is private. Up to 5,000 users are streamed as ndjson.

Path Parameters
teamIdCopy link to teamId
Type:string
required
Example
Query Parameters
fullCopy link to full
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Full user documents with performance ratings. This limits the response to 1,000 users.

Responses

Type:object
id
Type:string
required
Example

Type:string
required

Type:integer
Format:int64

Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
10

Join a team​Copy link
Join a team. If the team requires a password but the password field is incorrect, then the call fails with 403 Forbidden. Similarly, if the team join policy requires a confirmation but the message parameter is not given, then the call fails with 403 Forbidden.

Path Parameters
teamIdCopy link to teamId
Type:string
required
Example
Body
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
messageCopy link to message
Type:string
min length:  
30
max length:  
2000
Required if team manually reviews admission requests.

passwordCopy link to password
Type:string
Optional password, if the team requires one.

Responses
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
ok
Type:boolean
required
Request Example forpost/team/{teamId}/join
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/team/coders/join \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'message=' \
  --data-urlencode 'password='

Test Request
(post /team/{teamId}/join)
Status:200

{
  "ok": true
}
The request to join a team was successfully sent.

Board ​Copy link
Play on Lichess with physical boards and third-party clients. Works with normal Lichess accounts. Engine play or assistance is forbidden.

Features
Stream incoming chess moves
Play chess moves
Read and write in the player and spectator chats
Receive, create and accept (or decline) challenges
Abort and resign games
Compatible with normal Lichess accounts
Restrictions
Engine assistance, or any kind of outside help, is forbidden
Time controls: Rapid, Classical and Correspondence only. For direct challenges, games vs AI, and bulk pairing, Blitz is also possible.
Links
Announcement
Implementation example and live demo
Certabo support

Stream incoming events​Copy link
Stream the events reaching a lichess user in real time as ndjson.

An empty line is sent every 7 seconds for keep alive purposes.

Each non-empty line is a JSON object containing a type field. Possible values are:

gameStart Start of a game
gameFinish Completion of a game
challenge A player sends you a challenge or you challenge someone
challengeCanceled A player cancels their challenge to you
challengeDeclined The opponent declines your challenge
When the stream opens, all current challenges and games are sent.

Only one global event stream can be active at a time. When the stream opens, the previous one with the same access token is closed.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
The stream of events reaching the logged in user.

GameStartEvent
Create a seek​Copy link
Create a public seek, to start a game with a random player.

Real-time seek
Specify the time and increment clock values. The response is streamed but doesn't contain any information.

Keep the connection open to keep the seek active.

If the client closes the connection, the seek is canceled. This way, if the client terminates, the user won't be paired in a game they wouldn't play. When the seek is accepted, or expires, the server closes the connection.

Make sure to also have an Event stream open, to be notified when a game starts. We recommend opening the Event stream first, then the seek stream. This way, you won't miss the game event if the seek is accepted immediately.

Correspondence seek
Specify the days per turn value. The response is not streamed, it immediately completes with the seek ID. The seek remains active on the server until it is joined by someone.

Body
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
Parameters of the seek

colorCopy link to color
Type:string
enum
white
black
random
daysCopy link to days
Type:integer
enum
Days per turn. Required for correspondence seeks.

1
2
3
5
7
10
14
incrementCopy link to increment
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
180
Example
Clock increment in seconds. Required for real-time seeks.

ratedCopy link to rated
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Example
Whether the game is rated and impacts players ratings.

ratingRangeCopy link to ratingRange
Type:string
The rating range of potential opponents. Better left empty. Example: 1500-1800

timeCopy link to time
Type:number
min:  
0
max:  
180
Example
Clock initial time in minutes. Required for real-time seeks.

variantCopy link to variant
Type:string
enum
default: 
"standard"
Example
standard
chess960
crazyhouse
antichess
atomic
Show all values

200Copy link to 200
Type:object

Request Example forpost/api/board/seek
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/api/board/seek \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'rated=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'variant=standard' \
  --data-urlencode 'ratingRange=' \
  --data-urlencode 'time=15' \
  --data-urlencode 'increment=15' \
  --data-urlencode 'color=white'

Stream Board game state​Copy link
Stream the state of a game being played with the Board API, as ndjson.

Use this endpoint to get updates about the game in real-time, with a single request.

Each line is a JSON object containing a type field. Possible values are:

gameFull Full game data. All values are immutable, except for the state field.
gameState Current state of the game. Immutable values not included. Sent when a move is played, a draw is offered, or when the game ends.
chatLine Chat message sent by a user in the room "player" or "spectator".
opponentGone Whether the opponent has left the game, and how long before you can claim a win or draw.
The first line is always of type gameFull.

The server closes the stream when the game ends, or if the game has already ended.

Path Parameters
gameIdCopy link to gameId
Type:string
required
Example
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
The stream of the game.

Bot ​Copy link
Play on Lichess as a bot. Allows engine play. Read the blog post announcement of lichess bots.

Only works with Bot accounts.

Features
Stream incoming chess moves
Play chess moves
Read and write in the player and spectator chats
Receive, create and accept (or decline) challenges
Abort and resign games
Engine assistance is allowed
Restrictions
Bots can only play challenge games: pools and tournaments are off-limits
Bots cannot play UltraBullet (¼+0) because it requires making too many requests. But 0+1 and ½+0 are allowed.
Bots must follow Lichess TOS specifically Sandbagging, Constant Aborting, Boosting, etc
Bot devs are advised to make their Bots play casual only when testing their Bots logic and to avoid breaking Lichess TOS.
Integrations
Python3 lichess-bot (official)
Python3 lichess UCI bot
JavaScript bot-o-tron
Golang lichess-bot
Electronic Chessboard
Yours? Please make an issue or pull request.
Links
Announcement
Join the Lichess Bots team with your bot account
Get help in the discord channel
Watch Lichess Bot TV

Upgrade to Bot account​Copy link
Upgrade a lichess player account into a Bot account. Only Bot accounts can use the Bot API. The account cannot have played any game before becoming a Bot account. The upgrade is irreversible. The account will only be able to play as a Bot. To upgrade an account to Bot, use the official lichess-bot client, or follow these steps:

Create an API access token with "Play bot moves" permission.
curl -d '' https://lichess.org/api/bot/account/upgrade -H "Authorization: Bearer <yourTokenHere>" To know if an account has already been upgraded, use the Get my profile API: the title field should be set to BOT.
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
ok
Type:boolean
required
400Copy link to 400
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required
The cause of the error.

Stream Bot game state​Copy link
Stream the state of a game being played with the Bot API, as ndjson. Use this endpoint to get updates about the game in real-time, with a single request. Each line is a JSON object containing a type field. Possible values are:

gameFull Full game data. All values are immutable, except for the state field.
gameState Current state of the game. Immutable values not included.
chatLine Chat message sent by a user (or the bot itself) in the room "player" or "spectator".
opponentGone Whether the opponent has left the game, and how long before you can claim a win or draw. The first line is always of type gameFull.
Path Parameters
gameIdCopy link to gameId
Type:string
required
Example
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
The stream of the bot game.

GameFullEvent

Create a challenge​Copy link
Challenge someone to play. The targeted player can choose to accept or decline. If the challenge is accepted, you will be notified on the event stream that a new game has started. The game ID will be the same as the challenge ID. Challenges for realtime games (not correspondence) expire after 20s if not accepted. To prevent that, use the keepAliveStream flag described below.

Path Parameters
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
Example
Body
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
Parameters of the challenge

clock.incrementCopy link to clock.increment
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
60
Example
Clock increment in seconds. If empty, a correspondence game is created.

clock.limitCopy link to clock.limit
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
10800
Example
Clock initial time in seconds. If empty, a correspondence game is created. Valid values are 0, 15, 30, 45, 60, 90, and any multiple of 60 up to 10800 (3 hours).

colorCopy link to color
Type:string
enum
white
black
random
daysCopy link to days
Type:integer
enum
Days per move, for correspondence games. Clock settings must be omitted.

1
2
3
5
7
10
14
fenCopy link to fen
Type:string
default: 
"rnbqkbnr/pppppppp/8/8/8/8/PPPPPPPP/RNBQKBNR w KQkq - 0 1"
Custom initial position (in X-FEN). Variant must be standard, fromPosition, or chess960 (if a valid 960 starting position), and the game cannot be rated.

keepAliveStreamCopy link to keepAliveStream
Type:boolean
If set, the response is streamed as ndjson. The challenge is kept alive until the connection is closed by the client. When the challenge is accepted, declined or canceled, a message of the form {"done":"accepted"} is sent, then the connection is closed by the server. If not set, the response is not streamed, and the challenge expires after 20s if not accepted.

ratedCopy link to rated
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Game is rated and impacts players ratings

rulesCopy link to rules
Type:string
enum
Extra game rules separated by commas. Example: noAbort,noRematch

noAbort
noRematch
noGiveTime
noClaimWin
noEarlyDraw
variantCopy link to variant
Type:string
enum
default: 
"standard"
Example
standard
chess960
crazyhouse
antichess
atomic
Show all values
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example

  --request POST \

  --data-urlencode 'rated=false' \
  --data-urlencode 'color=white' \
  --data-urlencode 'variant=standard' \
  --data-urlencode 'fen=rnbqkbnr/pppppppp/8/8/8/8/PPPPPPPP/RNBQKBNR w KQkq - 0 1' \
  --data-urlencode 'keepAliveStream=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'rules=noAbort'

Cancel a challenge​Copy link
Cancel a challenge you sent, or aborts the game if the challenge was accepted, but the game was not yet played. Note that the ID of a game is the same as the ID of the challenge that created it. Works for user challenges and open challenges alike.

Path Parameters

Type:string
required
Example

opponentTokenCopy link to opponentToken
Type:string

Open-ended challenge​Copy link
Create a challenge that any 2 players can join. Share the URL of the challenge. the first 2 players to click it will be paired for a game. The response body also contains whiteUrl and blackUrl. You can control which color each player gets by giving them these URLs, instead of the main challenge URL. Open challenges expire after 24h. If the challenge creation is authenticated with OAuth2, then you can use the challenge cancel endpoint to cancel it. To directly pair 2 known players, use this endpoint instead.

Body
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
Parameters of the game

clock.incrementCopy link to clock.increment
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
60
Example

min:  
0
max:  
10800

Format:int64

default:

Custom initial position (in X-FEN). Variant must be standard, fromPosition, or chess960 (if a valid 960 starting position), and the game cannot be rated.

Start clocks of a game​Copy link
Start the clocks of a game immediately, even if a player has not yet made a move. Requires the OAuth tokens of both players with challenge:write scope. If the clocks have already started, the call will have no effect.

For AI games with only one player, omit the token2 parameter.

Path Parameters
gameIdCopy link to gameId
Type:string
required
ID of the game

Query Parameters
token1Copy link to token1
Type:string
required
OAuth token of a player

token2Copy link to token2
Type:string
OAuth token of the other player. Omit for AI games that have only one player.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
ok
Type:boolean
required

}

Admin challenge tokens​Copy link
This endpoint can only be used by Lichess administrators. It will not work if you do not have the appropriate permissions. Tournament organizers should instead use OAuth to obtain challenge:write tokens from users in order to perform bulk pairing.* Create and obtain challenge:write tokens for multiple users. If a similar token already exists for a user, it is reused. This endpoint is idempotent.

Create a bulk pairing​Copy link
Schedule many games at once, up to 24h in advance. OAuth tokens are required for all paired players, with the challenge:write scope. You can schedule up to 500 games every 10 minutes. Contact us if you need higher limits. If games have a real-time clock, each player must have only one pairing. For correspondence games, players can have multiple pairings within the same bulk.

The entire bulk is rejected if:

a token is missing
a token is present more than once (except in correspondence)
a token lacks the challenge:write scope
a player account is closed
a player is paired more than once (except in correspondence)
a bulk is already scheduled to start at the same time with the same player
you have 20 scheduled bulks
you have 1000 scheduled games
Partial bulks are never created. Either it all fails, or it all succeeds. When it fails, it does so with an error message explaining the issue. Failed bulks are not counted in the rate limiting, they are free. Fix the issues, manually or programmatically, then retry to schedule the bulk. A successful bulk creation returns a JSON bulk document. Its ID can be used for further operations.

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
Parameters of the pairings

clock.incrementCopy link to clock.increment
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
60
Clock increment in seconds. Example: 2

clock.limitCopy link to clock.limit
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
10800
Clock initial time in seconds. Example: 600

daysCopy link to days
Type:integer
enum
Days per turn. For correspondence games only.

1
2
3
5
7
10
14
fenCopy link to fen
Type:string
default: 
"rnbqkbnr/pppppppp/8/8/8/8/PPPPPPPP/RNBQKBNR w KQkq - 0 1"
Custom initial position (in X-FEN). Variant must be standard, fromPosition, or chess960 (if a valid 960 starting position), and the game cannot be rated.

messageCopy link to message
Type:string
default: 
"Your game with {opponent} is ready: {game}."
Message that will be sent to each player, when the game is created. It is sent from your user account. {opponent} and {game} are placeholders that will be replaced with the opponent and the game URLs. You can omit this field to send the default message, but if you set your own message, it must at least contain the {game} placeholder.

pairAtCopy link to pairAt
Type:integer
Format:int64
Date at which the games will be created as a Unix timestamp in milliseconds. Up to 7 days in the future. Omit, or set to current date and time, to start the games immediately. Example: 1612289869919

playersCopy link to players
Type:string
OAuth tokens of all the players to pair, with the syntax tokenOfWhitePlayerInGame1:tokenOfBlackPlayerInGame1,tokenOfWhitePlayerInGame2:tokenOfBlackPlayerInGame2,.... The 2 tokens of the players of a game are separated with :. The first token gets the white pieces. Games are separated with ,. Up to 1000 tokens can be sent, for a max of 500 games. Each token must be included at most once. Example: token1:token2,token3:token4,token5:token6

ratedCopy link to rated
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Game is rated and impacts players ratings

rulesCopy link to rules
Type:string
enum
Extra game rules separated by commas. Example: noAbort,noRematch

noAbort
noRematch
noGiveTime
noClaimWin
noEarlyDraw
startClocksAtCopy link to startClocksAt
Type:integer
Format:int64
Date at which the clocks will be automatically started as a Unix timestamp in milliseconds. Up to 7 days in the future. Note that the clocks can start earlier than specified, if players start making moves in the game. If omitted, the clocks will not start automatically. Example: 1612289869919

variantCopy link to variant
Type:string
enum
default: 
"standard"
Example
standard
chess960
crazyhouse
antichess
atomic
Show all values

Manually start clocks​Copy link
Immediately start all clocks of the games of a bulk pairing. This overrides the startClocksAt value of an existing bulk pairing. If the games have not yet been created (bulk.pairAt is in the future), then this does nothing. If the clocks have already started (bulk.startClocksAt is in the past), then this does nothing.

idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
Example
The ID of the bulk pairing

Responses
Show Headers

Type:object
ok
Type:boolean
required
404Copy link to 404
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required

Export games of a bulk pairing​Copy link
Download games of a bulk in PGN or ndjson format, depending on the request Accept header.

Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
Example
The ID of the bulk pairing

Query Parameters
movesCopy link to moves
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN moves.

pgnInJsonCopy link to pgnInJson
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the full PGN within the JSON response, in a pgn field.

tagsCopy link to tags
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN tags.

clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include clock status when available. Either as PGN comments: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] } Or in a clocks JSON field, as centisecond integers, depending on the response type.

evalsCopy link to evals
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include analysis evaluations and comments, when available. Either as PGN comments: 12. Bxf6 { [%eval 0.23] } a3 { [%eval -1.09] } Or in an analysis JSON field, depending on the response type.

accuracyCopy link to accuracy
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include accuracy percent of each player, when available. Only available in JSON.

openingCopy link to opening
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the opening name. Example: [Opening "King's Gambit Accepted, King's Knight Gambit"]

divisionCopy link to division
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Plies which mark the beginning of the middlegame and endgame. Only available in JSON

literateCopy link to literate
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Insert textual annotations in the PGN about the opening, analysis variations, mistakes, and game termination. Example: 5... g4? { (-0.98 → 0.60) Mistake. Best move was h6. } (5... h6 6. d4 Ne7 7. g3 d5 8. exd5 fxg3 9. hxg3 c6 10. dxc6)

Headers
AcceptCopy link to Accept
Type:string
enum
default: 
"application/x-chess-pgn"
Specify the desired response format. Use application/x-chess-pgn to get the games in PGN format. Use application/x-ndjson to get the games in ndjson format. Read about ndjson here and how you can parse it in Javascript.

application/x-chess-pgn
application/x-ndjson
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
The representation of the games.

  --header 'Accept: application/x-chess-pgn' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN'

Create a new Arena tournament​Copy link
Create a public or private Arena tournament. This endpoint mirrors the form on https://lichess.org/tournament/new. You can create up to 12 public tournaments per day, or 24 private tournaments. A team battle can be created by specifying the teamBattleByTeam argument. Additional restrictions:

clockTime + clockIncrement > 0
15s and 0+1 variant tournaments cannot be rated
Clock time in comparison to tournament length must be reasonable: 3 <= (minutes * 60) / (96 * clockTime + 48 * clockIncrement + 15) <= 150
Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
Parameters of the tournament

clockIncrementCopy link to clockIncrement
Type:integer
enum
required
Example
Clock increment in seconds

0
1
2
3
4
Show all values
clockTimeCopy link to clockTime
Type:number
enum
required
Example
Clock initial time in minutes

0
0.25
0.5
0.75
1
Show all values
minutesCopy link to minutes
Type:integer
enum
required
Example
How long the tournament lasts, in minutes

20
25
30
35
40
Show all values
berserkableCopy link to berserkable
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Whether the players can use berserk. Only allowed if clockIncrement <= clockTime * 2

conditions.accountAgeCopy link to conditions.accountAge
Type:integer
enum
Minium account age in days required to join.

1
3
7
14
30
Show all values
conditions.allowListCopy link to conditions.allowList
Type:string
Predefined list of usernames that are allowed to join, separated by commas. If this list is non-empty, then usernames absent from this list will be forbidden to join. Adding %titled to the list additionally allows any titled player to join. Example: thibault,german11,%titled

conditions.botsCopy link to conditions.bots
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Whether bots are allowed to join the tournament.

conditions.maxRating.ratingCopy link to conditions.maxRating.rating
Type:integer
enum
Maximum rating to join. Based on best rating reached in the last 7 days. Leave empty to let everyone join the tournament.

2200
2100
2000
1900
1800
Show all values
conditions.minRating.ratingCopy link to conditions.minRating.rating
Type:integer
enum
Minimum rating to join. Leave empty to let everyone join the tournament.

1000
1100
1200
1300
1400
Show all values
conditions.nbRatedGame.nbCopy link to conditions.nbRatedGame.nb
Type:integer
enum
Minimum number of rated games required to join.

0
5
10
15
20
Show all values
conditions.teamMember.teamIdCopy link to conditions.teamMember.teamId
Type:string
Restrict entry to members of a team. The teamId is the last part of a team URL, e.g. https://lichess.org/team/coders has teamId = coders. Leave empty to let everyone join the tournament. Do not use this to create team battles, use teamBattleByTeam instead.

descriptionCopy link to description
Type:string
Anything you want to tell players about the tournament

Request Example forpost/api/tournament
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/api/tournament \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'name=' \
  --data-urlencode 'clockTime=2' \
  --data-urlencode 'clockIncrement=1' \
  --data-urlencode 'minutes=60' \
  --data-urlencode 'waitMinutes=5' \
  --data-urlencode 'startDate=1' \
  --data-urlencode 'variant=standard' \
  --data-urlencode 'rated=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'position=rnbqkbnr/pppppppp/8/8/8/8/PPPPPPPP/RNBQKBNR w KQkq - 0 1' \
  --data-urlencode 'berserkable=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'streakable=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'hasChat=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'description=' \
  --data-urlencode 'password=' \
  --data-urlencode 'teamBattleByTeam=' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.teamMember.teamId=' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.minRating.rating=1000' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.maxRating.rating=2200' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.nbRatedGame.nb=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.allowList=' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.bots=false' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.accountAge=1'

(post /api/tournament)

Update an Arena tournament​Copy link
Update an Arena tournament. Be mindful not to make important changes to ongoing tournaments. Can be used to update a team battle. Additional restrictions:

clockTime + clockIncrement > 0
15s and 0+1 variant tournaments cannot be rated
Clock time in comparison to tournament length must be reasonable: 3 <= (minutes * 60) / (96 * clockTime + 48 * clockIncrement + 15) <= 150

Request Example forpost/api/tournament/{id}
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/tournament/{id}' \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'name=' \
  --data-urlencode 'clockTime=2' \
  --data-urlencode 'clockIncrement=1' \
  --data-urlencode 'minutes=60' \
  --data-urlencode 'waitMinutes=5' \
  --data-urlencode 'startDate=1' \
  --data-urlencode 'variant=standard' \
  --data-urlencode 'rated=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'position=rnbqkbnr/pppppppp/8/8/8/8/PPPPPPPP/RNBQKBNR w KQkq - 0 1' \
  --data-urlencode 'berserkable=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'streakable=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'hasChat=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'description=' \
  --data-urlencode 'password=' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.minRating.rating=1000' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.maxRating.rating=2200' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.nbRatedGame.nb=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.allowList=' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.bots=false' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.accountAge=1'

Join an Arena tournament​Copy link
Join an Arena tournament, possibly with a password and/or a team. Also unpauses if you had previously paused the tournament.

Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
Example
The tournament ID.

Body
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
You may need these depending on the tournament to join

pairMeAsapCopy link to pairMeAsap
Type:boolean
default: 
false
If the tournament is started, attempt to pair the user, even if they are not connected to the tournament page. This expires after one minute, to avoid pairing a user who is long gone. You may call "join" again to extend the waiting.

passwordCopy link to password
Type:string
The tournament password, if one is required. Can also be a user-specific entry code generated and shared by the organizer.

teamCopy link to team
Type:string
The team to join the tournament with, for team battle tournaments

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
ok
Type:boolean
required
400Copy link to 400
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required
The cause of the error.

Request Example forpost/api/tournament/{id}/join
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/api/tournament/hL7vMrFQ/join \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'password=' \
  --data-urlencode 'team=' \
  --data-urlencode 'pairMeAsap=false'

Test Request
(post /api/tournament/{id}/join)
Status:200
Status:400

{
  "ok": true
}
The tournament was successfully joined.

Export games of an Arena tournament​Copy link
Download games of a tournament in PGN or ndjson format. Games are sorted by reverse chronological order (most recent first). The game stream is throttled, depending on who is making the request:

Anonymous request: 20 games per second
OAuth2 authenticated request: 30 games per second
Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
The tournament ID.

Query Parameters
playerCopy link to player
Type:string
Only games of a particular player. Leave empty to fetch games of all players.

movesCopy link to moves
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN moves.

pgnInJsonCopy link to pgnInJson
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the full PGN within the JSON response, in a pgn field.

tagsCopy link to tags
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN tags.

clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include clock status when available. Either as PGN comments: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] } Or in a clocks JSON field, as centisecond integers, depending on the response type.

evalsCopy link to evals
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include analysis evaluations and comments, when available. Either as PGN comments: 12. Bxf6 { [%eval 0.23] } a3 { [%eval -1.09] } Or in an analysis JSON field, depending on the response type.

accuracyCopy link to accuracy
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include accuracy percent of each player, when available. Only available in JSON.

openingCopy link to opening
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the opening name. Example: [Opening "King's Gambit Accepted, King's Knight Gambit"]

divisionCopy link to division
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Plies which mark the beginning of the middlegame and endgame. Only available in JSON

Headers
AcceptCopy link to Accept
Type:string
enum
default: 
"application/x-chess-pgn"
Specify the desired response format. Use application/x-chess-pgn to get the games in PGN format. Use application/x-ndjson to get the games in ndjson format. Read about ndjson here and how you can parse it in Javascript.

application/x-chess-pgn
application/x-ndjson
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
The list of games of an Arena tournament.

Request Example forget/api/tournament/{id}/games
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/tournament/{id}/games?player=&moves=true&pgnInJson=false&tags=true&clocks=false&evals=false&accuracy=false&opening=false&division=false' \
  --header 'Accept: application/x-chess-pgn'

Test Request
(get /api/tournament/{id}/games)
Status:200

The list of games of an Arena tournament.

Get results of an Arena tournament​Copy link
Players of an Arena tournament, with their score and performance, sorted by rank (best first). Players are streamed as ndjson, i.e. one JSON object per line. If called on an ongoing tournament, results can be inconsistent due to ranking changes while the players are being streamed. Use on finished tournaments for guaranteed consistency.

Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
The tournament ID.

Query Parameters
nbCopy link to nb
Type:integer
min:  
1
Max number of players to fetch

sheetCopy link to sheet
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Add a sheet field to the player document. It's an expensive server computation that slows down the stream.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
performance
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

rank
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

rating
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

score
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

username
Type:string
required
flair
Type:string
See available flair list and images

patronColor
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
10
Players can choose a color for their Patron wings. See here for the color mappings.

The presence of this field indicates the player is an active Patron.

Type:object

Get tournaments created by a user​Copy link
Get all tournaments created by a given user. Tournaments are sorted by reverse chronological order of start date (last starting first). Tournaments are streamed as ndjson. The stream is throttled, depending on who is making the request:

Anonymous request: 20 tournaments per second
OAuth2 authenticated request: 30 tournaments per second
Authenticated, downloading your own tournaments: 50 tournaments per second
Path Parameters
usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
required
The user whose created tournaments to fetch

Query Parameters
nbCopy link to nb
Type:integer
min:  
1
Max number of tournaments to fetch
