Type:integer
enum
Include tournaments in the given status: "Created" (10), "Started" (20), "Finished" (30) You can add this parameter more than once to include tournaments in different statuses. Example: ?status=10&status=20

20
30

Create a new Swiss tournament​Copy link
Create a Swiss tournament for your team. This endpoint mirrors the Swiss tournament form from your team pagee. You can create up to 12 tournaments per day. Additional restrictions:

clock.limit + clock.increment > 0
15s and 0+1 variant tournaments cannot be rated
Path Parameters
teamIdCopy link to teamId
Type:string
required
ID of the team

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
Parameters of the tournament

clock.incrementCopy link to clock.increment
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
120
required
Example
Clock increment in seconds

clock.limitCopy link to clock.limit
Type:integer
enum
required
Example
Clock initial time in seconds

0
15
30
45
60
Show all values
nbRoundsCopy link to nbRounds
Type:integer
min:  
3
max:  
100
required
Maximum number of rounds to play

chatForCopy link to chatFor
Type:integer
enum
default: 
20
Who can read and write in the chat.

0 = No-one
10 = Only team leaders
20 = Only team members
30 = All Lichess players
0
10
20
30
conditions.allowListCopy link to conditions.allowList
Type:string
Predefined list of usernames that are allowed to join, separated by commas. If this list is non-empty, then usernames absent from this list will be forbidden to join. Adding %titled to the list additionally allows any titled player to join. Example: thibault,german11,%titled

conditions.maxRating.ratingCopy link to conditions.maxRating.rating
Type:integer
enum
Maximum rating to join. Based on best rating reached in the last 7 days. Leave empty to let everyone join the tournament.

2200
2100
2000
1900
1800
Show all values
conditions.minRating.ratingCopy link to conditions.minRating.rating
Type:integer
enum
Minimum rating to join. Leave empty to let everyone join the tournament.

1000
1100
1200
1300
1400
Show all values
conditions.nbRatedGame.nbCopy link to conditions.nbRatedGame.nb
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
200
Minimum number of rated games required to join.

conditions.playYourGamesCopy link to conditions.playYourGames
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Only let players join if they have played their last swiss game. If they failed to show up in a recent swiss event, they won't be able to enter yours. This results in a better swiss experience for the players who actually show up.

descriptionCopy link to description
Type:string
Anything you want to tell players about the tournament

forbiddenPairingsCopy link to forbiddenPairings
Type:string
Usernames of players that must not play together. Two usernames per line, separated by a space.

manualPairingsCopy link to manualPairings
Type:string
Manual pairings for the next round. Two usernames per line, separated by a space. Example:

PlayerA PlayerB
PlayerC PlayerD
To give a bye (1 point) to a player instead of a pairing, add a line like so:

PlayerE 1
Missing players will be considered absent and get zero points.

Request Example forpost/api/swiss/new/{teamId}
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/swiss/new/{teamId}' \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'name=' \
  --data-urlencode 'clock.limit=300' \
  --data-urlencode 'clock.increment=1' \
  --data-urlencode 'nbRounds=3' \
  --data-urlencode 'startsAt=1' \
  --data-urlencode 'roundInterval=-1' \
  --data-urlencode 'variant=standard' \
  --data-urlencode 'position=rnbqkbnr/pppppppp/8/8/8/8/PPPPPPPP/RNBQKBNR w KQkq - 0 1' \
  --data-urlencode 'description=' \
  --data-urlencode 'rated=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'password=' \
  --data-urlencode 'forbiddenPairings=' \
  --data-urlencode 'manualPairings=' \
  --data-urlencode 'chatFor=20' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.minRating.rating=1000' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.maxRating.rating=2200' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.nbRatedGame.nb=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.playYourGames=false' \
  --data-urlencode 'conditions.allowList='

Manually schedule the next round​Copy link
Manually schedule the next round date and time of a Swiss tournament. This sets the roundInterval field to 99999999, i.e. manual scheduling. All further rounds will need to be manually scheduled, unless the roundInterval field is changed back to automatic scheduling.

Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
Example
The tournament ID.

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
Parameters of the tournament

dateCopy link to date
Type:integer
Format:int64
Timestamp in milliseconds to start the next round at a given date and time.

Responses
Show Headers
204Copy link to 204
The Swiss tournament was successfully updated.

400Copy link to 400
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required
The cause of the error.

401Copy link to 401
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string

Export TRF of a Swiss tournament​Copy link
Download a tournament in the Tournament Report File format, the FIDE standard. Documentation: https://www.fide.com/FIDE/handbook/C04Annex2_TRF16.pdf Example: https://lichess.org/swiss/j8rtJ5GL.trf

Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
The tournament ID.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
The TRF representation of a Swiss tournament.

Request Example forget/swiss/{id}.trf
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/swiss/{id}.trf'

Test Request
(get /swiss/{id}.trf)
Status:200

string
The TRF representation of a Swiss tournament.

Export games of a Swiss tournament​Copy link
Download games of a swiss tournament in PGN or ndjson format. Games are sorted by chronological order. The game stream is throttled, depending on who is making the request:

Anonymous request: 20 games per second
OAuth2 authenticated request: 30 games per second
Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
The tournament ID.

Query Parameters
playerCopy link to player
Type:string
Only the games played by a given player

movesCopy link to moves
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN moves.

pgnInJsonCopy link to pgnInJson
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the full PGN within the JSON response, in a pgn field.

tagsCopy link to tags
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include the PGN tags.

clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include clock status when available. Either as PGN comments: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] } Or in a clocks JSON field, as centisecond integers, depending on the response type.

evalsCopy link to evals
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include analysis evaluations and comments, when available. Either as PGN comments: 12. Bxf6 { [%eval 0.23] } a3 { [%eval -1.09] } Or in an analysis JSON field, depending on the response type.

accuracyCopy link to accuracy
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include accuracy percent of each player, when available. Only available in JSON.

openingCopy link to opening
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Include the opening name. Example: [Opening "King's Gambit Accepted, King's Knight Gambit"]

divisionCopy link to division
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Plies which mark the beginning of the middlegame and endgame. Only available in JSON

Headers
AcceptCopy link to Accept
Type:string
enum
default: 
"application/x-chess-pgn"
Specify the desired response format. Use application/x-chess-pgn to get the games in PGN format. Use application/x-ndjson to get the games in ndjson format. Read about ndjson here and how you can parse it in Javascript.

application/x-chess-pgn
application/x-ndjson
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
The list of games of a Swiss tournament.

Request Example forget/api/swiss/{id}/games
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/swiss/{id}/games?player=&moves=true&pgnInJson=false&tags=true&clocks=false&evals=false&accuracy=false&opening=false&division=false' \
  --header 'Accept: application/x-chess-pgn'

Test Request
(get /api/swiss/{id}/games)
Status:200

[Event "Rated Blitz game"]
[Site "https://lichess.org/fY44h4OY"]
[Date "2018.03.29"]
[Round "-"]
[White "pveldman"]
[Black "thibault"]
[Result "1-0"]
[UTCDate "2018.03.29"]
[UTCTime "01:38:15"]
[WhiteElo "1610"]
[BlackElo "1601"]
[WhiteRatingDiff "+10"]
[BlackRatingDiff "-10"]
[Variant "Standard"]
[TimeControl "180+0"]
[ECO "C62"]
[Opening "Ruy Lopez: Steinitz Defense"]
[Termination "Normal"]

1. e4 { [%clk 0:03:00] } e5 { [%clk 0:03:00] } 2. Nf3 { [%clk 0:02:59] } Nc6 { [%clk 0:02:58] } 3. Bb5 { [%clk 0:02:57] } d6 { [%clk 0:02:55] } 4. h3 { [%clk 0:02:54] } Nf6 { [%clk 0:02:52] } 5. Bxc6+ { [%clk 0:02:52] } bxc6 { [%clk 0:02:49] } 6. d3 { [%clk 0:02:51] } Be7 { [%clk 0:02:46] } 7. O-O { [%clk 0:02:47] } O-O { [%clk 0:02:45] } 8. b3 { [%clk 0:02:45] } d5 { [%clk 0:02:45] } 9. exd5 { [%clk 0:02:33] } cxd5 { [%clk 0:02:40] } 10. Nxe5 { [%clk 0:02:31] } Qd6 { [%clk 0:02:38] } 1-0
The list of games of a Swiss tournament.

Get results of a swiss tournament​Copy link
Players of a swiss tournament, with their score and performance, sorted by rank (best first). Players are streamed as ndjson. If called on an ongoing tournament, results can be inconsistent due to ranking changes while the players are being streamed. Use on finished tournaments for guaranteed consistency.

Path Parameters
idCopy link to id
Type:string
required
The tournament ID.

Query Parameters
nbCopy link to nb
Type:integer
min:  
1
Max number of players to fetch

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
performance
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

points
Type:number
required
rank
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

rating
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

tieBreak
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

username
Type:string
required
absent
Type:boolean
title
Type:string
enum
only appears if the user is a titled player or a bot user

GM
WGM

WIM
FM
Show all values

The results of a Swiss tournament.

Get team swiss tournaments​Copy link
Get all swiss tournaments of a team. Tournaments are sorted by reverse chronological order of start date (last starting first). Tournaments are streamed as ndjson.

Path Parameters
teamIdCopy link to teamId
Type:string
required
Example
Query Parameters
maxCopy link to max
Type:integer
min:  
1
default: 
100
How many tournaments to download.

statusCopy link to status
Type:string
enum
[Filter] Only swiss tournaments in this current state.

created
started
finished
createdByCopy link to createdBy
Type:string
[Filter] Only swiss tournaments created by a given user.

nameCopy link to name
Type:string
[Filter] Only swiss tournaments with a given name.

Simuls ​Copy link
Access simuls played on Lichess. https://lichess.org/simul

SimulsOperations
get
/api/simul
Get current simuls​Copy link
Get recently created, started, finished, simuls. Created and finished simul lists are not exhaustives, only those with strong enough host will be listed, the same filter is used to display simuls on https://lichess.org/simul. When authenticated with OAuth2, the pending list will be populated with your created, but unstarted simuls.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
created
Type:array Simul[]
Show Child Attributesfor created
finished
Type:array Simul[]
Show Child Attributesfor finished
pending
Type:array Simul[]
Show Child Attributesfor pending
started
Type:array Simul[]
Show Child Attributesfor started

Studies ​Copy link
Access Lichess studies. https://lichess.org/study

StudiesOperations

/api/study/{studyId}/{chapterId}.pgn

/api/study/{studyId}.pgn

/api/study/{studyId}.pgn

get
/api/study/by/{username}

/api/study/{studyId}/{chapterId}
Export one study chapter​Copy link
Download one study chapter in PGN format. If authenticated, then all public, unlisted, and private study chapters are read. If not, only public (non-unlisted) study chapters are read.

Path Parameters
studyIdCopy link to studyId
Type:string
min length:  
8
max length:  
8
required
The study ID

chapterIdCopy link to chapterId
Type:string
min length:  
8
max length:  
8
required
The chapter ID

Query Parameters
clocksCopy link to clocks
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include clock comments in the PGN moves, when available. Example: 2. exd5 { [%clk 1:01:27] } e5 { [%clk 1:01:28] }

commentsCopy link to comments
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include analysis and annotator comments in the PGN moves, when available. Example: 12. Bxf6 { [%eval 0.23] } a3 { White is in a pickle. }

variationsCopy link to variations
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Include non-mainline moves, when available. Example: 4. d4 Bb4+ (4... Nc6 5. Nf3 Bb4+ 6. Bd2 (6. Nbd2 O-O 7. O-O) 6... Bd6) 5. Nd2

orientationCopy link to orientation
Type:boolean
default: 
false
Add a Orientation PGN tag with the chapter predefined orientation. Example: [Orientation "white"]

Responses
200Copy link to 200
Type:string

The chapter of the study.

[Event "All about the Sicilian Defense: Dragon Variation"]
[Site "https://lichess.org/study/8c8bmUfy/qwnXMwVC"]
[Result "*"]
[UTCDate "2017.06.25"]
[UTCTime "10:12:04"]
[Variant "Standard"]
[ECO "B76"]
[Opening "Sicilian Defense: Dragon Variation, Yugoslav Attack, Panov Variation"]
[Annotator "https://lichess.org/@/Francesco_Super"]

{ This chapter will go over the Dragon Variation, a very common variation used by Black and it is the most aggressive variation in the Sicilian defense. }
1. e4 c5 2. Nf3 { Simple developing move to control the d4 square } { [%csl Gd4,Gc5][%cal Gf3d4,Gc5d4] } 2... d6 { [%cal Gd6e5] } (2... e6 3. d4 cxd4 4. Nxd4 Nf6 5. e5 (5. Nc3 { [%cal Ge4e5] }) 5... Qa5+) 3. d4 { Whites want the exchange of pawns } { [%cal Gc5d4] } 3... cxd4 { [%cal Gf3d4] } 4. Nxd4 { Whites are now ahead in development but blacks still have the two central pawns whereas whites only one. } { [%csl Ge7,Gd6,Ge4] } 4... Nf6 { Blacks are now developing their knight and threatening the e4 pawn } { [%csl Ge4][%cal Gf6e4] } 5. Nc3 { The e4 pawn is now protected by the c3 knight } { [%csl Ge4,Bc3][%cal Rf6e4,Bc3e4] } 5... g6 { This is the DRAGON VARIATION. g6 allows the dark-squared bishop to develop and move to g7, controlling the long dark-squared diagonal } { [%csl Gd4] } 6. Be3 { [%cal Gd1d2,Gf2f3,Ge1c1,Gg2g4,Gh2h4,Gg4g5] } (6. Be2 Bg7 7. O-O Nc6 8. Be3 { [%cal Ge3d4] } (8. f3 Nxe4 { [%cal Gg7d4,Gc6d4] } 9. Nxc6 Qb6+ { [%cal Gb6c6,Gb6g1] } 10. Kh1 Nxc3 { [%cal Gc3d1,Gc3e2] } 11. bxc3 bxc6 { [%cal Gc8a6] }) 8... O-O 9. Nb3 a6 { [%cal Gb7b5,Gb5b4,Ge2c4] }) 6... Bg7 (6... Ng4 { [%cal Gg4e3] } 7. Bb5+ { [%cal Gb5e8,Gb8d7,Gc8d7,Gd1g4] } 7... Nc6 8. Nxc6 bxc6 9. Bxc6+ { [%cal Gc6a8] }) 7. f3 { The key opening moves for White, who attempt to castle queenside , whereas f3 strengthens the pawn structure, connecting e4 to the h2 and g2, while White also plan pushing to g4 and possibly h4. } { [%csl Bf3,Be3][%cal Rg2g4,Rh2h4,Rg4g5] } 7... O-O (7... h5 { Is operating against g4. }) 8. Qd2 { [%csl Gh6,Gg7][%cal Ge1c1,Ga1d1,Re3h6,Rd2h6] } 8... Nc6 { [%csl Gc6,Gh6][%cal Gb8c6,Ge1c1,Ga7a6,Ge3h6] } 9. g4 (9. Bh6 { [%cal Ge3d4] } 9... Bxh6 10. Qxh6 Nxd4) 9... Be6 10. Nxe6 fxe6 { [%cal Gf8f1] } 11. O-O-O Ne5 12. Be2 { [%csl Gf3][%cal Re5f3,Bd1h1,Bg1d1] } 12... Qc7 { [%csl Gc4][%cal Ge5c4,Gc4e3,Gc4d2,Bf8c8,Yc7c3] } 13. h4 Nc4 *

Import PGN into a study​Copy link
Imports arbitrary PGN into an existing study. Creates a new chapter in the study. If the PGN contains multiple games (separated by 2 or more newlines) then multiple chapters will be created within the study. Note that a study can contain at most 64 chapters.

Path Parameters
studyIdCopy link to studyId
Type:string
required
ID of the study

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
Parameters of the import

pgnCopy link to pgn
Type:string
required
PGN to import. Can contain multiple games separated by 2 or more newlines.

nameCopy link to name
Type:string
min length:  
1
max length:  
100
Name of the new chapter. If not specified, or if multiple chapters are created, the names will be inferred from the PGN tags.

orientationCopy link to orientation
Type:string
enum
default: 
"white"
Default board orientation.

white
black
variantCopy link to variant
Type:string
enum
default: 
"standard"
Example
standard
chess960
crazyhouse
antichess
atomic
Show all values
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
chapters
Type:array object[]
Show Child Attributesfor chapters
400Copy link to 400
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required
The cause of the error.

Request Example forpost/api/study/{studyId}/import-pgn
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/study/{studyId}/import-pgn' \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'pgn=' \
  --data-urlencode 'name=' \
  --data-urlencode 'orientation=white' \
  --data-urlencode 'variant=standard'

Update PGN tags of a study chapter​Copy link
Add, update and delete the PGN tags of a study. By providing a list of PGN tags in the usual PGN format, you can:

Add new tags if the chapter doesn't have them yet
Update existing chapter tags
Delete existing chapter tags, by providing a tag with an empty value.
The chapter keeps the tags that you don't provide.

Path Parameters
studyIdCopy link to studyId
Type:string
min length:  
8
max length:  
8
required
The study ID

chapterIdCopy link to chapterId
Type:string
min length:  
8
max length:  
8
required
The chapter ID

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
pgnCopy link to pgn
Type:string
required
PGN text containing the tags. Only the tags are used. Moves are just ignored.

Responses
Show Headers
204Copy link to 204
Tags updated successfully, if the chapter exists and you are authorized the update the study.

400Copy link to 400
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required
The cause of the error.

Request Example forpost/api/study/{studyId}/{chapterId}/tags
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/study/{studyId}/{chapterId}/tags' \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'pgn='

(post /api/study/{studyId}/{chapterId}/tags)

Status:400
No Body

Broadcasts ​Copy link
Relay chess events on Lichess. Official broadcasts are maintained by Lichess, but you can create your own broadcasts to cover any live game or chess event. You will need to publish PGN on a public URL so that Lichess can pull updates from it. Alternatively, you can push PGN updates to Lichess using this API endpoint.

Broadcasts are organized in tournaments, which have several rounds, which have several games. You must first create a tournament, then you can add rounds to them.

BroadcastsOperations
get
/api/broadcast
get
/api/broadcast/top
get
/api/broadcast/by/{username}
get
/api/broadcast/search
post
/broadcast/new
get
/api/broadcast/{broadcastTournamentId}
get
/broadcast/{broadcastTournamentId}/players
get
/broadcast/{broadcastTournamentId}/players/{playerId}
post
/broadcast/{broadcastTournamentId}/edit
post
/broadcast/{broadcastTournamentId}/new
get
/api/broadcast/{broadcastTournamentSlug}/{broadcastRoundSlug}/{broadcastRoundId}
post
/broadcast/round/{broadcastRoundId}/edit
post
/api/broadcast/round/{broadcastRoundId}/reset
post
/api/broadcast/round/{broadcastRoundId}/push
get
/api/stream/broadcast/round/{broadcastRoundId}.pgn
get
/api/broadcast/round/{broadcastRoundId}.pgn
get
/api/broadcast/{broadcastTournamentId}.pgn
get
/api/broadcast/my-rounds
Get official broadcasts​Copy link
Returns ongoing official broadcasts sorted by tier. After that, returns finished broadcasts sorted by most recent sync time. Broadcasts are streamed as ndjson.

Query Parameters

Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
100
default:

Create a broadcast tournament​Copy link
Create a new broadcast tournament to relay external games. This endpoint accepts the same form data as the web form.

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
nameCopy link to name
Type:string
min length:  
3
max length:  
80
required
Name of the broadcast tournament.

Example: Sinquefield Cup

info.fideTcCopy link to info.fideTc
Type:string
enum
FIDE rating category. Which FIDE ratings to use

standard
rapid
blitz
info.formatCopy link to info.format
Type:string
max length:  
80
Tournament format. Example: "8-player round-robin" or "5-round Swiss"

info.locationCopy link to info.location
Type:string
max length:  
80
Tournament Location

info.playersCopy link to info.players
Type:string
max length:  
120
Mention up to 4 of the best players participating.

info.standingsCopy link to info.standings
Type:string
Format:uri
Official Standings. External website URL, e.g. chess-results.com, info64.org

info.tcCopy link to info.tc
Type:string
max length:  
80
Time control. Example: "Classical" or "Rapid" or "Rapid & Blitz"

info.timeZoneCopy link to info.timeZone
Type:string
Timezone of the tournament. Example: America/New_York. See list of possible timezone identifiers for more.

info.websiteCopy link to info.website
Type:string
Format:uri
Official website. External website URL

markdownCopy link to markdown
Type:string
max length:  
20000
Optional long description of the broadcast. Markdown is supported.

playersCopy link to players
Type:string
Optional replace player names, ratings and titles.

One line per player, formatted as such:

player name / FIDE ID
Example:

Magnus Carlsen / 1503014
Player names ignore case and punctuation, and match all possible combinations of 2 words: "Jorge Rick Vito" will match "Jorge Rick", "jorge vito", "Rick, Vito", etc.

If the player is NM or WNM, you can:

player name / FIDE ID / title
Alternatively, you may set tags manually, like so:

player name / rating / title / new name
All values are optional. Example:

Magnus Carlsen / 2863 / GM
YouGotLittUp / 1890 / / Louis Litt
showRatingDiffsCopy link to showRatingDiffs
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Show player's rating diffs

Show additional propertiesfor Request Body
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
rounds
Type:array BroadcastRoundInfo[]
required
Show Child Attributesfor rounds
tour
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor tour
defaultRoundId
Type:string
group
Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor group
400Copy link to 400
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required
The cause of the error.

Request Example forpost/broadcast/new
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/broadcast/new \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'name=' \
  --data-urlencode 'info.format=' \
  --data-urlencode 'info.location=' \
  --data-urlencode 'info.tc=' \
  --data-urlencode 'info.fideTc=standard' \
  --data-urlencode 'info.timeZone=' \
  --data-urlencode 'info.players=' \
  --data-urlencode 'info.website=' \
  --data-urlencode 'info.standings=' \
  --data-urlencode 'markdown=' \
  --data-urlencode 'showScores=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'showRatingDiffs=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'teamTable=false' \
  --data-urlencode 'visibility=public' \
  --data-urlencode 'players=' \
  --data-urlencode 'teams=' \
  --data-urlencode 'tier=3' \
  --data-urlencode 'tiebreaks%5B%5D=AOB'

Test Request
(post /broadcast/new)
Status:200
Status:400

{
  "tour": {
    "id": "nceYXagc",
    "name": "Knight Invitational",
    "slug": "knight-invitational",
    "info": {},
    "createdAt": 1764375024906,
    "url": "https://lichess.org/broadcast/knight-invitational/nceYXagc",
    "tier": 5
  },
  "rounds": []
}
The broadcast tournament was successfully created.

Create a broadcast round​Copy link
Create a new broadcast round to relay external games. This endpoint accepts the same form data as the web form.

Choose one between syncUrl, syncUrls, syncIds and syncUsers, if it is missing, the broadcast needs to be fed by pushing PGN to it

Path Parameters
broadcastTournamentIdCopy link to broadcastTournamentId
Type:string
min length:  
8
max length:  
8
required
The broadcast tournament ID

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
customScoring.black.drawCopy link to customScoring.black.draw
Type:number
min:  
0
max:  
10
customScoring.black.winCopy link to customScoring.black.win
Type:number
min:  
0
max:  
10
customScoring.white.drawCopy link to customScoring.white.draw
Type:number
min:  
0
max:  
10
customScoring.white.winCopy link to customScoring.white.win
Type:number
min:  
0
max:  
10
delayCopy link to delay
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
3600
Delay in seconds for movements to appear on the broadcast. Leave it empty if you don't need it. Example: 900 (15 min)

nameCopy link to name
Type:string
min length:  
3
max length:  
80
Name of the broadcast round. Example: Round 1

onlyRoundCopy link to onlyRound
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
999
Filter games by round number

Optional, only keep games from the source that match a round number. It uses the PGN Round tag. These would match round 3:

[Round "3"]
[Round "3.1"]
If you set a round number, then games without a Round tag are dropped.

It only works if you chose syncUrl or syncUrls as the source.

periodCopy link to period
Type:integer
min:  
2
max:  
60
(Only for Admins) Waiting time for each poll.

ratedCopy link to rated
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Whether the round is used when calculating players' rating changes.

slicesCopy link to slices
Type:string
Select slices of the games

Optional. Select games based on their position in the source.

1           only select the first board
1-4         only select the first 4 boards
1,2,3,4     same as above, first 4 boards
11-15,21-25 boards 11 to 15, and boards 21 to 25
2,3,7-9     boards 2, 3, 7, 8, and 9
Slicing is done after filtering by round number.

It only works if you chose syncUrl or syncUrls as the source.

startsAfterPreviousCopy link to startsAfterPrevious
Type:boolean
default: 
false
The start date is unknown, and the round will start automatically when the previous round completes.

startsAtCopy link to startsAt
Type:integer
Format:int64
min:  
1356998400070
Timestamp in milliseconds of broadcast round start. Leave empty to manually start the broadcast round. Example: 1356998400070

statusCopy link to status
Type:string
enum
default: 
"new"
Lichess can usually detect the round status, but you can also set it manually if needed.

new
started
finished
syncIdsCopy link to syncIds
Type:string
Lichess game IDs - Up to 100 Lichess game IDs, separated by spaces.

syncSourceCopy link to syncSource
Type:string
enum
default: 
"push"
Where the games come from.

push
url
urls
ids
users
syncUrlCopy link to syncUrl
Type:string
Format:uri
URL that Lichess will poll to get updates about the games. It must be publicly accessible from the Internet.

Example:

https://myserver.org/myevent/round-10/games.pgn
syncUrlsCopy link to syncUrls
Type:string
URLs that Lichess will poll to get updates about the games, separated by newlines. They must be publicly accessible from the Internet.

Example:

https://myserver.org/myevent/round-10/game-1.pgn
https://myserver.org/myevent/round-10/game-2.pgn
syncUsersCopy link to syncUsers
Type:string
Up to 100 Lichess usernames, separated by spaces

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
round
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor round
study
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor study
tour
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor tour
400Copy link to 400
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required
The cause of the error.

Request Example forpost/broadcast/{broadcastTournamentId}/new
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/broadcast/{broadcastTournamentId}/new' \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN' \
  --data-urlencode 'name=' \
  --data-urlencode 'syncSource=push' \
  --data-urlencode 'startsAt=1356998400070' \
  --data-urlencode 'startsAfterPrevious=false' \
  --data-urlencode 'delay=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'status=new' \
  --data-urlencode 'rated=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'customScoring.white.win=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'customScoring.white.draw=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'customScoring.black.win=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'customScoring.black.draw=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'period=2'

Regular Scoring
Update a broadcast round​Copy link
Update information about a broadcast round. This endpoint accepts the same form data as the web form. All fields must be populated with data. Missing fields will override the broadcast with empty data. For instance, if you omit startDate, then any pre-existing start date will be removed.

Path Parameters
broadcastRoundIdCopy link to broadcastRoundId
Type:string
min length:  
8
max length:  
8
required
The broadcast round ID

Query Parameters
patchCopy link to patch
Type:boolean
Example
Only update the provided fields, leaving others unchanged

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
customScoring.black.drawCopy link to customScoring.black.draw
Type:number
min:  
0
max:  
10
customScoring.black.winCopy link to customScoring.black.win
Type:number
min:  
0
max:  
10
customScoring.white.drawCopy link to customScoring.white.draw
Type:number
min:  
0
max:  
10
customScoring.white.winCopy link to customScoring.white.win
Type:number
min:  
0
max:  
10
delayCopy link to delay
Type:integer
min:  
0
max:  
3600
Delay in seconds for movements to appear on the broadcast. Leave it empty if you don't need it. Example: 900 (15 min)

nameCopy link to name
Type:string
min length:  
3
max length:  
80
Name of the broadcast round. Example: Round 1

onlyRoundCopy link to onlyRound
Type:integer
min:  
1
max:  
999
Filter games by round number

Optional, only keep games from the source that match a round number. It uses the PGN Round tag. These would match round 3:

[Round "3"]
[Round "3.1"]
If you set a round number, then games without a Round tag are dropped.

It only works if you chose syncUrl or syncUrls as the source.

periodCopy link to period
Type:integer
min:  
2
max:  
60
(Only for Admins) Waiting time for each poll.

ratedCopy link to rated
Type:boolean
default: 
true
Whether the round is used when calculating players' rating changes.

slicesCopy link to slices
Type:string
Select slices of the games

Optional. Select games based on their position in the source.

1           only select the first board
1-4         only select the first 4 boards
1,2,3,4     same as above, first 4 boards
11-15,21-25 boards 11 to 15, and boards 21 to 25
2,3,7-9     boards 2, 3, 7, 8, and 9
Slicing is done after filtering by round number.

It only works if you chose syncUrl or syncUrls as the source.

startsAfterPreviousCopy link to startsAfterPrevious
Type:boolean
default: 
false
The start date is unknown, and the round will start automatically when the previous round completes.

startsAtCopy link to startsAt
Type:integer
Format:int64
min:  
1356998400070
Timestamp in milliseconds of broadcast round start. Leave empty to manually start the broadcast round. Example: 1356998400070

statusCopy link to status
Type:string
enum
default: 
"new"
Lichess can usually detect the round status, but you can also set it manually if needed.

new
started
finished
syncIdsCopy link to syncIds
Type:string
Lichess game IDs - Up to 100 Lichess game IDs, separated by spaces.

syncSourceCopy link to syncSource
Type:string
enum
default: 
"push"
Where the games come from.

push
url
urls
ids
users
syncUrlCopy link to syncUrl
Type:string
Format:uri
URL that Lichess will poll to get updates about the games. It must be publicly accessible from the Internet.

Example:

https://myserver.org/myevent/round-10/games.pgn
syncUrlsCopy link to syncUrls
Type:string
URLs that Lichess will poll to get updates about the games, separated by newlines. They must be publicly accessible from the Internet.

Example:

https://myserver.org/myevent/round-10/game-1.pgn
https://myserver.org/myevent/round-10/game-2.pgn
syncUsersCopy link to syncUsers
Type:string
Up to 100 Lichess usernames, separated by spaces

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
games
Type:array BroadcastRoundGame[]
required
Show Child Attributesfor games

Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor round

required
Show Child Attributesfor study

Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor tour

Type:object
Show Child Attributesfor group

Type:boolean
Indicates if the user making the request is subscribed to the broadcast

400Copy link to 400
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required
The cause of the error.

  --data-urlencode 'syncSource=push' \
  --data-urlencode 'startsAt=1356998400070' \
  --data-urlencode 'startsAfterPrevious=false' \
  --data-urlencode 'delay=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'status=new' \
  --data-urlencode 'rated=true' \
  --data-urlencode 'customScoring.white.win=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'customScoring.white.draw=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'customScoring.black.win=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'customScoring.black.draw=0' \
  --data-urlencode 'period=2'

Stream an ongoing broadcast round as PGN​Copy link
This streaming endpoint first sends all games of a broadcast round in PGN format. Then, it waits for new moves to be played. As soon as it happens, the entire PGN of the game is sent to the stream. The stream will also send PGNs when games are added to the round. This is the best way to get updates about an ongoing round. Streaming means no polling, and no pollings means no latency, and minimum impact on the server.

Path Parameters
broadcastRoundIdCopy link to broadcastRoundId
Type:string
min length:  
8
max length:  
8
required
The broadcast round ID

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
Example
The PGN representation of the round games, then the PGNs of games as they are updated.

Request Example forget/api/stream/broadcast/round/{broadcastRoundId}.pgn
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/api/stream/broadcast/round/{broadcastRoundId}.pgn'

(get /api/stream/broadcast/round/{broadcastRoundId}.pgn)

Export one round as PGN​Copy link
Download all games of a single round of a broadcast tournament in PGN format. You could poll this endpoint to get updates about a tournament, but it would be slow, and very inefficient. Instead, consider streaming the tournament to get a new PGN every time a game is updated, in real-time.

Path Parameters
broadcastRoundIdCopy link to broadcastRoundId
Type:string
min length:  
8
max length:  
8
required
The round ID

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:string
Example
Example
The PGN representation of the round.

Get your broadcast rounds​Copy link
Stream all broadcast rounds you are a member of. Also includes broadcasts rounds you did not create, but were invited to. Also includes broadcasts rounds where you're a non-writing member. See the writeable flag in the response. Rounds are ordered by rank, which is roughly chronological, most recent first, slightly pondered with popularity.

Query Parameters
nbCopy link to nb
Type:integer
min:  
1
Example
How many rounds to get

Responses
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
round
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor round
study
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor study
tour
Type:object
required
Show Child Attributesfor tour

Analysis ​Copy link
Access Lichess cloud evaluations database. https://lichess.org/analysis

AnalysisOperations
get
/api/cloud-eval
Get cloud evaluation of a position.​Copy link
Get the cached evaluation of a position, if available. Opening positions have more chances of being available. There are about 320 million positions in the database. Up to 5 variations may be available. Variants are supported. Use this endpoint to fetch a few positions here and there. If you want to download a lot of positions, get the full list from our exported database.

Query Parameters
fenCopy link to fen
Type:string
required
Example
X-FEN of the position

multiPvCopy link to multiPv
Type:integer
default: 
1
Number of variations

variantCopy link to variant
Type:string
enum
default: 
"standard"
Example
Variant

standard
chess960
crazyhouse
antichess
atomic
Show all values
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
depth
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

fen
Type:string
required
knodes
Type:integer
required
Integer numbers.

pvs
Type:array object[]
required
Show Child Attributesfor pvs
404Copy link to 404
Type:object
error
Type:string

Tablebase ​Copy link
Lookup positions from the Lichess tablebase server.

The endpoint hostname is not lichess.org but tablebase.lichess.ovh.

TablebaseOperations
get
/standard
get
/atomic
get
/antichess
Tablebase lookup​Copy link
Endpoint: https://tablebase.lichess.ovh

Example: curl http://tablebase.lichess.ovh/standard?fen=4k3/6KP/8/8/8/8/7p/8_w_-_-_0_1

Query Parameters
fenCopy link to fen
Type:string
required
X-FEN of the position. Underscores allowed.

dtcCopy link to dtc
Type:string
enum
When to query the tablebase for dtc values. The current default is never. It is eventually going to be auxiliary, i.e., only when the position is not covered by one of the other tablebases.

never
auxiliary
always
Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
Example
category
Type:string
enum
required
cursed-win and blessed-loss means the 50-move rule prevents the decisive result.

syzygy-win and syzygy-loss means exact result is unknown due to DTZ rounding, i.e., the win or loss could also be prevented by the 50-move rule if the user has deviated from the tablebase recommendation since the last pawn move or capture.

maybe-win and maybe-loss means the result with regard to the 50-move rule is unknown, because DTZ is unknown and the DTC tablebase does not guarantee to reach a zeroing move as soon as possible.

win
unknown
syzygy-win
maybe-win
cursed-win
Show all values
moves
Type:array TablebaseMove[]
required
Information about legal moves, best first

Show Child Attributesfor moves
checkmate
Type:boolean
dtc
Type:null | integer
Experimental Depth to Conversion: Moves to next capture, promotion, or checkmate. Available for:

Standard chess positions with 8 pieces, more than one pawn of material value for each side, and at least one pair of opposing pawns, short op1, if query parameter dtc is auxiliary or always.
Some standard chess positions with up to 7 pieces, if query parameter dtc is always. Work in progress.
dtm
Type:null | integer
Depth To Mate: Plies to mate (available only for Standard positions with not more than 5 pieces)

dtw
Type:null | integer
Depth To Win: Plies to win (available only for Antichess positions with not more than 4 pieces)

dtz
Type:null | integer
DTZ50'' with rounding in plies (for Standard chess positions with not more than 7 pieces and variant positions not more than 6 pieces)

insufficient_material
Type:boolean
precise_dtz
Type:null | integer
DTZ50'' in plies, only if guaranteed to not be rounded, or absent if unknown

stalemate
Type:boolean
variant_loss
Type:boolean
Only in chess variants

variant_win
Type:boolean
Only in chess variants

Request Example forget/standard
Shell Curl

curl 'https://tablebase.lichess.ovh/standard?fen=&dtc=never'

The tablebase information for the position in atomic chess.

Tablebase lookup for Antichess​Copy link
Endpoint: https://tablebase.lichess.ovh

Query Parameters
fenCopy link to fen
Type:string
required
X-FEN of the position. Underscores allowed.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
Example
category
Type:string
enum
required
cursed-win and blessed-loss means the 50-move rule prevents the decisive result.

syzygy-win and syzygy-loss means exact result is unknown due to DTZ rounding, i.e., the win or loss could also be prevented by the 50-move rule if the user has deviated from the tablebase recommendation since the last pawn move or capture.

maybe-win and maybe-loss means the result with regard to the 50-move rule is unknown, because DTZ is unknown and the DTC tablebase does not guarantee to reach a zeroing move as soon as possible.

win
unknown
syzygy-win
maybe-win
cursed-win
Show all values
moves
Type:array TablebaseMove[]
required
Information about legal moves, best first

Show Child Attributesfor moves
checkmate
Type:boolean
dtc
Type:null | integer
Experimental Depth to Conversion: Moves to next capture, promotion, or checkmate. Available for:

Standard chess positions with 8 pieces, more than one pawn of material value for each side, and at least one pair of opposing pawns, short op1, if query parameter dtc is auxiliary or always.
Some standard chess positions with up to 7 pieces, if query parameter dtc is always. Work in progress.
dtm
Type:null | integer
Depth To Mate: Plies to mate (available only for Standard positions with not more than 5 pieces)

dtw
Type:null | integer
Depth To Win: Plies to win (available only for Antichess positions with not more than 4 pieces)

dtz
Type:null | integer
DTZ50'' with rounding in plies (for Standard chess positions with not more than 7 pieces and variant positions not more than 6 pieces)

insufficient_material
Type:boolean
precise_dtz
Type:null | integer
DTZ50'' in plies, only if guaranteed to not be rounded, or absent if unknown

stalemate
Type:boolean
variant_loss
Type:boolean
Only in chess variants

variant_win
Type:boolean
Only in chess variants

Request Example forget/antichess
Shell Curl

curl 'https://tablebase.lichess.ovh/antichess?fen='

OAuth ​Copy link
Obtaining and revoking OAuth tokens.

Read about the Lichess API authentication methods and code examples.

OAuthOperations
get
/oauth
post
/api/token
delete
/api/token
post
/api/token/test
Request authorization code​Copy link
OAuth2 authorization endpoint. Start the OAuth2 Authorization Code Flow with PKCE by securely generating two random strings unique to each authorization request:

code_verifier
state
Store these in session storage. Make sure not to reveal code_verifier to eavesdroppers. Do not show it in URLs, do not abuse state to store it, do not send it over insecure connections. However it is fine if the user themselves can extract code_verifier, which will always be possible for fully client-side apps. Then send the user to this endpoint. They will be prompted to grant authorization and then be redirected back to the given redirect_uri. If the authorization failed, the following query string parameters will be appended to the redirection:

error, in particular with value access_denied if the user cancelled authorization
error_description to aid debugging
state, exactly as passed in the state parameter
If the authorization succeeded, the following query string parameters will be appended to the redirection:

code, containing a fresh short-lived authorization code
state, exactly as passed in the state parameter
Next, to defend against cross site request forgery, check that the returned state matches the state you originally generated.

Finally, continue by using the authorization code to obtain an access token.

Query Parameters
response_typeCopy link to response_type
const:  
code
required
Must be code.

client_idCopy link to client_id
Type:string
required
Example
Arbitrary identifier that uniquely identifies your application.

redirect_uriCopy link to redirect_uri
Type:string
required
The absolute URL that the user should be redirected to with the authorization result.

code_challenge_methodCopy link to code_challenge_method
const:  
S256
required
Must be S256.

code_challengeCopy link to code_challenge
Type:string
required
Compute BASE64URL(SHA256(code_verifier)).

scopeCopy link to scope
Type:string
Space separated list of requested OAuth scopes, if any.

usernameCopy link to username
Type:string
Hint that you want the user to log in with a specific Lichess username.

stateCopy link to state
Type:string
Arbitrary state that will be returned verbatim with the authorization result.

Responses
200Copy link to 200
Authorization prompt will be displayed to the user.

Request Example forget/oauth
Shell Curl

curl 'https://lichess.org/oauth?response_type=code&client_id=example.com&redirect_uri=&code_challenge_method=S256&code_challenge=&scope=&username=&state='

Test Request
(get /oauth)
Status:200
No Body
Authorization prompt will be displayed to the user.

Obtain access token​Copy link
OAuth2 token endpoint. Exchanges an authorization code for an access token.

Body
required
application/x-www-form-urlencoded
client_idCopy link to client_id
Type:string
Example
Must match the client_id used to request the authorization code.

codeCopy link to code
Type:string
Example
The authorization code that was sent in the code parameter to your redirect_uri.

code_verifierCopy link to code_verifier
Type:string
Example
A code_challenge was used to request the authorization code. This must be the code_verifier it was derived from.

grant_typeCopy link to grant_type
const:  
authorization_code
Example
redirect_uriCopy link to redirect_uri
Type:string
Example
Must match the redirect_uri used to request the authorization code.

Responses
Show Headers
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
access_token
Type:string
required
Example
expires_in
Type:integer
required
Example
Integer numbers.

token_type
Type:string
required
Example
Show Headers
400Copy link to 400
Type:object
Example
error
Type:string
required
The cause of the error.

error_description
Type:string
The reason why the request was rejected.

Request Example forpost/api/token
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/api/token \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --data-urlencode 'grant_type=authorization_code' \
  --data-urlencode 'code=liu_iS1uOZg99Htmo58ex2jKgYziUfzsnAl0' \
  --data-urlencode 'code_verifier=Ry1rbGdOMTQtUjhOc0lmTnFKak1LTHV0NjlRMll2aXYtTThkQnlJRkRpaGwyQjh0ZDNFdzFPSG9KUlY4M1NrRzJ5ZHhUdjVZR08zLTZOT3dCN2xLfjZOXzU2WHk4SENP' \
  --data-urlencode 'redirect_uri=http://example.com/' \
  --data-urlencode 'client_id=example.com'

Revoke access token​Copy link
Revokes the access token sent as Bearer for this request.

Responses
Show Headers
204Copy link to 204
Access token revoked.

Request Example fordelete/api/token
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/api/token \
  --request DELETE \
  --header 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_SECRET_TOKEN'

Test Request
(delete /api/token)
Status:204
No Body
Access token revoked.

Test multiple OAuth tokens​Copy link
For up to 1000 OAuth tokens, returns their associated user ID and scopes, or null if the token is invalid. The method is POST so a longer list of tokens can be sent in the request body.

Body
required
text/plain
OAuth tokens separated by commas. Up to 1000.

Type:string
Responses
200Copy link to 200
Type:object
Example
token
Type:object
nullable
expires
Type:integer | null
Unix-timestamp in milliseconds or null if the token never expires.

scopes
Type:string
Comma-separated list of scopes. Empty string if the token has no scopes.

userId
Type:string
Request Example forpost/api/token/test
Shell Curl

curl https://lichess.org/api/token/test \
  --request POST \
  --header 'Content-Type: text/plain' \
  --data '"lip_jose,lip_badToken\n"'

Test Request
(post /api/token/test)
Status:200

{
  "lip_jose": {
    "userId": "jose",
    "scopes": "preference:read,preference:write,email:read,challenge:read,challenge:write,challenge:bulk,study:read,study:write,tournament:write,racer:write,puzzle:read,puzzle:write,team:read,team:write,team:lead,follow:read,follow:write,msg:write,board:play,bot:play,engine:read,engine:write,web:login,web:mod",
    "expires": null
  },
  "lip_badToken": null
}
The representation of the OAuth tokens.
